skyabs @# / /
'gro sems bskyed tshad med bzhi sgom brgyud dang 'dres nges pa sngon du btang la /

gsol /

blo bzang rgyal kun mkhyen brtse'i 'od dkar gyis / /

mkhyen dang brtse ba'i ye shes 'od snang gis / /
ma lus skye dgu'i mun pa sel mdzad pa'i / /
bshes gnyen @# / /
nyin byed dbang bo zhabs brtan shog /
blo bzang rgyal ba gnyis pa'i gzhung lugs mchog /
ji bzhin 'byed la mi 'jigs spobs pa can / /
ye shes mtshan ldan 'gro ba'i gnyen gcig bu / /
rje btsun bla ma srid mthar zhabs brtan shog /
blo bzang rgyal bstan dri med 'od dkar gyis / /
dad ldan gdul bya'i kun+da'i tshal bzhad cing / /
ye shes zer gyis 'gro ba'i mi shes mun / /
sel mdzad rje btsun bla ma zhabs brtan shog /
blo gsal skal ldan yongs kyi cod pan la / /
ches dkar mdzad bzang gom ba 'god mkhas pa / /
ye shes mtshan can 'gro ba'i mig gcig pu / /
dpal ldan bla ma yun ring zhabs brtan shog /
blo bzang rgyal ba'i ring lugs sbel ba la / /
mkhas mang rgya mtsho'i gtsug na mngon par brjid / /
gzhung lugs kun la ye shes spyan yangs pa / /
dpal ldan bla ma srid mthar zhabs brtan shog /
de ltar rtse gcig gsol ba btab pa'i mthus / /
gangs ri'i ra bas rab mdzes zhing khams 'dir phan bde'i 'byung gnas dpal ldan bla ma yi / /
zhabs kyi padma yun ring brtan par shog /
bslu med dkon mchog rin chen byin rlabs dang / /
drang srong rig sngags grub pa'i bden tshig dang / /
bstan srungs dam can rgya mtsho'i mthu rtsal gyis /
rje btsun bla ma bskal brgyar zhabs brtan shog /
ces pa 'di ni dga' ldan phun tshogs gling pa'i rdo rje slob dpon dang dbu chos sogs kyis ring 'tsho'i tshigs bcad tshogs 'don du bcugs chog pa zhig dgos zhes bskul ba ltar shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras ba'o / /
! na mo gu ru many+dzu g+ho ShA ya /
blo bzang ye shes mchog gis bde ba cher / /
rol bas sku gsum go 'phang mngon gyur pa / /
rgyal ba gnyis pa'i bstan pa rgyas mdzad pa'i / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
he ru ka dngos blo bzang grags pa yi / /
bstan pa'i gsal byed ye shes 'od snang gis / /
sa gsum 'gro ba'i mun ba sel mdzad pa'i / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo chen spyod pa bzang pos lha yi lam / /
cig car khyab mdzad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyis / /
dad ldan gdul bya'i pad tshal 'byed ba'i gnyen / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
de ltar mos blos gsol ba btab pa'i mthus / /
chos brgyad spros pa'i khol por mi 'gyur zhing / /
rtse gcig sgrub pa snying po lhur blangs bas / /
bla ma he ru ka yis rjes 'dzin shog /
mdor na bdag gi dge ba ji snyed pa / /
nyam thag 'gro ba 'di kun srid mtsho las / /
sgrol phyir rim gnyis rtogs pa mngon gyur te / /
tshe gcig sangs rgyas thob pa'i rgyu ru bsngo /
zhes pa 'di ni a mdo bla ma blo bzang chos skyong gis bskul ba ltar /
chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa 'gro kun he ru kas rjes su 'dzin pa'i rgyur gyur cig /
bkra shis / /
! swasti /
blo bzang grags bstan 'chi med rgyal mtshan gyis / /
tshangs pa'i yul sa'i bar du khyab mdzad cing / /
mkhas btsun yon tan tog gis rab mdzes pa'i / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol @# / /
ba 'debs / /
mdo sngags tshig don ma lus 'chad ba yis / /
gdul bya thar 'dod lam du 'dren mdzad cing / /
bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin la zla bral ba / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo bzang 'phrin las ye shes 'od bo ches / /
mtha' b+khob mun ba'i smag rum sel mdzad cing / /
skal bzang gdul bya'i padmo'i tshal 'byed pa'i / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
dkon mchog gsum gyi bden pa'i byin rlabs dang / /
rig sngags 'chang ba'i bden mthu rnam dag dang / /
bstan srungs dam can rgya mtsho'i mthu rtsal gyis / /
'gro 'dren skyabs mgon dam ba zhabs brtan shog /
blo bzang chos kyi mdun sa'i dga' tshal cher / /
legs bshad mkhas mang dbus su sgrog ba la / /
zla mod rnam dpyod spobs ba mngon mtho ba / /
lha mi'i 'dren mchog yun ring zhabs brtan shog /
de ltar dad dang gus bas gsol btab mthus / /
skye ba 'di dang tshe rabs thams cad du / /
rje btsun bla mas 'bral med rjes bzungs te / /
bka' bzhin sgrub ba snying por byed par shog /
tshe rabs kun tu bla ma lha mchog la / /
gsol ba legs bar btab pa'i byin rlabs kyis / /
rjes bzungs gsung gi chos kyi skal bzang la / /
ngoms pa med par rgyun du spyod par shog /
ces pa 'di ni dge slong chos mdzad kyis bskul ba ltar / /
chos smra ba'i btsun ba blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa dge legs 'phel / /
! oM swasti /
bde stong dbyer med lha yi lam yangs por / /
rin chen sna tshogs kyis spras khri yi steng / /
sna tshogs padma nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor dbus / /
bka' drin gsum ldan rtsa ba'i bla ma dang / /
dbyer med rgyal ba'i yab gcig 'jam pa'i dbyangs / /
sku mdog nyi ma 'char ka'i mdangs lta bu / /
bcu drug lo lon gzhon sha chags pa'i sku / /
zhal gcig phyag gnyis glegs bam ral gris mtshan / /
sgeg cing 'dzum pa'i nyams ldan zur phud 'chang / /
rin chen cod ban sna tshogs dar gyis klubs / /
yid 'phrog 'ja' tshon sna lnga'i gur khyim dbus / /
rdo rje skyil krung tshul gyis bzhugs pa yi / /
spyi bor oM dkar mgrin par AHdmar po / /
thugs kar hUM sngon hUM yig 'od zer gyis / /
ngang bzhin gnas nas rtsa ba'i bla ma dang / /
dbyer med ye shes spyan drangs ro gcig gyur / /
phyag 'tshal mchod cing nyes ltung ma lus bshags / /
rang gzhan rnam dkar kun la rjes yi rang / /
chos 'khor bskor phyir srid mthar rtag bzhugs gsol / /
'dis mtshon dge ba rdzogs byang rgyu ru bsngo / /
rgyal kun mkhyen brtse'i gter chen ngag gi lha / /
dur smrig gar gyis rnam rol sbrul pa'i sku / /
snyigs dus 'gro ba kun gyi skyabs gcig pu / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
'phags pa'i nor bdun yon tan gyis phyug cing / /
rgyal bstan mi nub 'dzin la zla bral zhing / /
chos kun ma lus mngon sum gzigs ba yi / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
mchog gsum bslu med bden pa'i byin rlabs dang @# / /
bstan srungs dam can rgya mtsho'i mthu stobs dang / /
skal ldan 'gro ba yongs kyis gsol btab mthus / /
lha mi'i 'dren ba bskal brgyar zhabs brtan shog /
de ltar rtse gcig gsol ba btab ba'i mthus / /
tshe rabs kun tu theg mchod dge ba'i bshes / /
mgon bo khyod kyis 'bral med rjes bzungs nas / /
gsung gi bdud rtsi ngoms med 'thung bar shog /
gnas skabs su yang phyi nang 'tshe ba kun / /
nyer zhi dam chos tshul bzhin sgrub ba yi / /
mthun rkyen ma lus yid bzhin 'grub ba dang / /
rgyal bstan mi nub phyogs mthar rgyas byed shog /
ces ba 'di ni dge slong ngag dbang stobs ldan gyis bskul ba la brten nas chos smra ba'i btsun ba blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras ba'o / /
mang+galaM / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
'chi med lam yangs mchod sprin 'khrigs ba'i dbus / /
gnyis 'thung dbang pos legs bteg rin chen khrir / /
chu skyes nyi zla rgyas ba'i dkyil 'khor steng / /
bka' drin gsum ldan rtsa ba'i bla ma ni / /
rnam dag dge slong tshul bzungs sku mdog dkar / /
zhal gcig phyag gnyis chos 'chad mnyam gzhag steng / /
bdud rtsis gang ba'i drang srong snod mchog bsnams / /
gser gyi mdangs ldan paN zhwa rab mdzes shing / /
dur smrig mdog can chos gos bsum gyis klubs / /
'od zer stong 'bar gur khyim 'khrigs ba'i dbus / /
dgyes shing 'dzum pa'i nyams chags gzi 'od 'bar / /
rdo rje skyil krung tshul gyis legs par bzhugs /
de yi dpral bar dI baM ka ra dang / /
mgrin par rgyal ba gnyis ba tsong kha ba / /
snying gar paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan ni / /
ye shes sems dpa'i tshul du brtan par bzhugs / /
mtha' skor brgyud ba'i bla ma yi dam dang / /
sangs rgyas byang sems dpa' bo mkha' 'gro dang / /
gang la gang 'dul sna tshogs skur ston pa'i / /
bstan srungs rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyis gang bar bzhugs / /
gnas gsum yi ge gsum mtshan 'od zer gyis / /
rang bzhin gnas nas ye shes sems dba' rnams / /
sbyan drangs rang rang dam tshig sems dpa' dang / /
dbyer med dgyes ba'i tshul gyi bzhugs par gyur / /
phyag 'tshal mchod cing sdig ltung ma lus bshags / /
skyon bral mdzad pa kun la yi rang zhing / /
'gro la chos 'khor bskor phyir rtag bzhugs gsol / /
'dis mtshon rnam dkar byang chub chen bor bsngo / /
blo bzang rgyal bstan 'dzin la mngon mtho zhing / /
ye shes 'od kyis gdul bya'i rmongs mun sel / /
rlabs chen mdzad pas phyogs kun khyab pa yi / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
rmad byung bslu med mchog gsum byin rlabs dang / /
dam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyi mthu stobs dang / /
mos ldan skye dgus rtse gcig gsol btab mthus / /
rje btsun bla ma srid mthar zhabs brtan shog /
de ltar gus pa'i yid kyis gsol btab mthus / /
skye ba kun tu dpal ldan bla ma dang / /
skad cig tsam yang nam yang mi 'bral zhing / /
theg mchog dam ba'i chos la spyod par shog /
yul @# / /
phyogs 'dir yang dbal 'byor mi nyams shing / /
mi mthun nyer 'tshe ma lus zhi ba dang / /
khams gsum chos kyi rgyal bo tsong kha ba'i / /
bstan pa phyogs mthar rgyas ba'i bkra shis shog /
ces ba'i di ni dga' ldan chos gling gi bla ma dka' bcu blo bzang rgyal mtshan gyi 'dod ba bzhin /
shAkya'i btsun ba blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa'o / /
mang+galaM / /
! oM sa ma ya tAShTHi / /
mi zad ngag gi 'dod 'jo 'jam ba'i dbyangs ma rungs 'dul phyir gshin rje'i skur bstan ba / /
'jigs mdzad dba' bo chen po la btud nas / /
gnyer gtad g.yel ba med pa'i dam tshig brjod / /
dbal ldan myur mdzad mgon po phyag drug ba / /
yab yum gtum drag 'khor tshogs rgya mtsho dang / /
legs nyes shan 'byed chos kyi rgyal bo ni / /
'chi bdag bka' nyan pho mo'i chogs dang bcas / /
srid gsum bdag mo snyigs dus gdul dka' ba / /
'dul mdzad mo rgyud bstan srungs tshogs rnams dang /
gu gyi mgon po dbal ldan phyag bzhi ba / /
zhing skyong gzi ldan yum chen sring mo bzhi / /
'gri thogs bshan pa'i tshogs kyis bskor ba dang / /
dregs ba lcam srid 'khor dang bcas pa sogs / /
snying ma'i dus 'dir rdo rje 'chang dbang gis / /
gnyer du gtad ba'i chos srungs mtha' dag la / /
chos grwa che 'dir gsar du bkod pa yi / /
rnam dag gzhal med khang 'dra'i mchod khang rnams / /
rgyal dang rgyal sras sku gsung thugs kyi rten / /
byin rlabs gzi byin 'phro ba ji snyed dang / /
phyogs bcu dag nas yongs 'dus mchod ba'i rdzas / /
rmad byung dpag yas dam rdzas sbyan gzigs chags / /
bcol lo gtad do ma g.yel bdag mdzad nas / /
'di dag rnams las rdul phran tsam zhig kyang / /
'jabs bus rku dang stobs kyis 'khyer ba sogs / /
bsam sbyor ngan pa'i sems 'chad ma lus ba / /
drag pos tshar chong snying khrag zhal du gsol / /
bkra shis lhun gyis grub ba'i gtsug lag khang / /
dge 'dun sde bcas rten gsum mchod rdzas rnams / /
nam yang srung skyob g.yel ba med par mdzod / /
sa ma ya tIShTHa /
zhes ba 'di ni gshin rje'i gshed kyi rnal 'byor pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bstan ba'i rgyun la phan par bsams nas bkod ba'o / /
mang+galaM / /
! oM sa ma ya tIShTHa /
lha chen drag bo dpal ldan zhal bzhi ba / /
yum bzhi gri thogs bshan pa 'khor bcas dang / /
'dod khams dbang phyug dmag zor re ma ti / /
mo rgyud sangs rgyas bstan srungs tshogs rnams la grwa 'di'i dge 'dun sde dang phyi nang gi /
nor dang longs spyod dpal 'byor ma lus ba / /
bcol lo gtad do srung skyob ma g.yel bar / /
yar ngo'i zla ltar 'phel zhing rgyas par mdzod /
sarba mang+galaM / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
blo bzang rgyal ba'i bstan la rab zhugs nas / /
thos bsam sgom la brtson pa lhur len cing / /
skal bzang gdul bya'i re ba skong ba yi / /
ye shes mtshan can zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
'khor lo gsum dang bshad sgrub bya ba @# / /
yis / /
rgyal ba gnyis ba'i bstan ba 'dzin ba'i dpal / /
'phrin las 'od zer phyogs bcur 'phro ba can / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo gros bzang bo'i ba gam mthon po nas / /
'gro la brtse ba'i ye shes 'od stong 'phro / /
dad ldan gdul bya'i pad tshal rgyas mdzad ba'i / /
bstan pa'i nyi ma mchog la gsol ba 'debs / /
lhag bsam rnam dag rtsa ba rab brtan cing / /
tshad med bzhi yi bang rim mngon par mtho / /
don gnyis lhun grub lcog gis rab mdzes ba'i / /
bshes gnyen ri dbang mchog la gsol ba 'debs / /
thub bstan kai la sha yi ri bo nas / /
legs par 'ongs ba'i dam chos gang+ga'i rgyun / /
rnam dpyod blo gros rgya mtshor legs 'khyil ba'i / /
yongs 'dzin dam ba'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
rgyal ba gnyis pa'i ring lugs shing rta che / /
lhag bsam stobs kyis 'dren la zla bral zhing / /
'gro la 'dod dgu'i mchog sbyin mdzad pa yi / /
bshes gnyen dam ba'i mgon la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo chen rgyal sras rnams kyi mkhyen ba'i dbyid / /
bzang po'i mdzad pas 'gro ba smin mdzad cing / /
ye shes 'od kyis rmongs ba kun sel ba'i / /
thub bstan nyin mo'i mgon la gsol ba 'debs / /
mthong bas yid 'phrog mtshan dpe 'bar ba'i sku / /
rna bar snyan 'jebs chos sgra sgrog ba'i gsung / /
zab yangs blo gros gting dpag dka' ba'i thugs / /
'gro ba'i 'dren ba mchog la gsol ba 'debs / /
mdo rgyud tshig don 'chad la thogs med cing / /
rtsod bas pha rol rgol bzil gyis gnon / /
rtsom pas mkhas pa kun gyi yid 'phrog pa'i / /
mkhyen rab dbang phyug zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo gros bzang bo'i dzam bu br-Ik+Sha'i rtser / /
bslab gsum 'bras /
bu'i khur gyis g.yur za zhing / /
mi 'dad tsha gdung sel ba'i gri ba bsil can / /
bshes gnyen dpag bsam dbang bor gsol ba 'debs / /
smon 'jug thig pa chen por sems bskyed cing / /
rgyal sras rlabs chen spyod ba'i bya ba yis / /
'gro rnams smin grol lam la 'god mdzad ba'i / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba'i debs / /
gdong lnga 'bar bas bteg pa'i khri 'phang rtser / /
bskal brgya'i bar du g.yo ba med bzhugs nas / /
rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha ba'i / /
ring lugs chad ba med par spel bar shog /
bslu med bla ma yi dam byin rlabs dang / /
bstan srungs dam can rgya mtsho'i mthu stobs kyis / /
kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i bstan pa'i gnyen gcig pu / /

'gro la phan bde ma lus 'byung ba'i gzhi / /

thub pa'i bstan @# / /
la rab byung thos bsam gyis / /
legs par dul zhing bag yod bya ba yis / /
rnam dag bcas pa'i mtshams las g.yel med shog /
rnam g.yeng le los nam yang mi bskyod ba'i / /
ting 'dzin mchog la rtag tu yid gzhol zhing so sor rtog ba'i shes rab zab mo yis / /
srid pa'i rtsa ba ma lus drungs 'byin shog /
'gro la brtse ba'i byams dang snying rje yis / /
theg chen rigs kyi bag chags yongs sad de / /
smon 'jug byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed nas / /
phyin drug spyod bas nyin mtshan 'da' bar shog /
de ltar thun mong lam gyis rgyud spyangs nas / /
sku bzhi'i sa bon thebs ba'i dbang bzhi yis / /
gsang sngags zab mo'i sgo 'phar legs phye nas / /
dam tshig sdom pa srog ltar gces 'dzin shog /
de nas rim gnyis zab mo'i rnal 'byor la / /
rtse gcig mnyam bar 'jog pa'i ting 'dzin gyis / /
tha mal snang zhen 'khrul brgyad bsrings te / /
tshe gcig nyid la zung 'jug mchog thob shog /
mdor na dam chos sgrub pa'i mi mthun phyogs / /
mi shis mtshan mnye bar zhi ba dang / /
dbal ldan bla ma'i 'phrin las dar zhing rgyas / /
'gro kun bde la spyod ba'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di ni dge slong don grub rgyal mtshan gyis bskul ba'i ngor chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis nyi 'od 'khyil par sug bris su bgyis pa mang+galaM / /
! na mo many+dzu g+ho ShA ya /
blo bzang rgyal ba gnyis pa'i lung rtogs kyi / /
bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i dpal gyur cing / /
mtha' yas gdul bya'i bsod nams zhing gi mchag /
rje btsun sprul pa'i sku la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo chen rgyal sras kun gyi mdzad ba'i phul / /
gdul dka' 'dul phyir bzang po'i mdzad ba can / /
mkhas dang grub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i mchog /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi thugs rje dang / /
bslu med rten 'brel dam chos bden ba dang / /
rig grol gnyis ldan 'phags pa'i byin rlabs kyis / /
bstan ba'i rgyal mtshan rtag tu g.yo med shog /
gzungs dang ting 'dzin mthu la dbang 'byor ba'i / /
drang srong grub ba'i smon lam bden tshig dang / /
dad ldan gdul byas gsol ba btab ba'i mthus / /
bstan 'dzin dam pa bskal brgyar zhabs brtan shog /
de ltar gdung ba'i yid kyis gsol btab mthus / /
deng nas yang srid skye ba thams cad du / /
rje btsun bla mas 'bral med rjes bzungs nas / /
dam chos dga' ba de'i dpal la rol par shog /
ces rje btsun dam ba 'jam dbyangs sprul pa'i sku'i gsol 'debs brtan bzhugs dang bcas pa 'di ni kun dga' bkra shis kyis bskul bltar chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis gzims khang rgyal mtshan mthon po'i nyi 'od 'khyil bar sbyar ba dge legs 'phel / /
! swasti /
mkhyen ba'i ye shes dkyil 'khor 'od stong can tshogs gnyis rgya mtsho'i klong las legs 'thon pa / /
blo gsal gdul bya'i pad tshal rgyas mdzad pa'i / /
yongs 'dzin dam pa'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs /
zhes dkyil khang zhal snga nas ye shes rgya mtsho'i sku bstong bla rgyud gsol 'debs @# / /
su bton chog ba zhig dgos zhes shud khung rab 'byams ba dge 'dun dpal 'byor gyis bskul ba ltar chos smra ba'i btsun ba blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa sarba dza yan+tu / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
rmad byung bkod legs rin chen yol go 'di / /
mdo rgyud smra ba blo bzang chos 'dzin dang / /
spyi mi las byed rnams kyis khur blangs shing / /
lho bod 'ga' yis mthun rkyen sbyar te bsgrubs / /
'di ltar bgyis pa'i rnam dkar phung po'i mthus / /
blo bzang rgyal bstan 'dab brgya padmo'i gnyen / /
nam mkha'i nor bu ye shes 'od 'bar ba / /
bskal brgya'i bar du g.yo med ches gsal zhing / /
sde 'dir dpal 'byor bshad sgrub 'phel ba dang / /
tshul 'di sgrub la sgo gsum ci rigs kyis /
mthun rkyen sgrub pa'i lus can ma lus kyang / /
bsam don ji bzhin 'bad med 'grub bar shog /
phun tshogs 'dod dgu'i g.yang chags snod mchog 'di / /

de la 'dir sku 'bum byams pa gling gi dgon sde chen po 'di nyid ni khams gsum chos kyi rgyal bo tsong kha pa chen po blta mas ba'i sar tsan+dan gyi ljon ba zhig 'khrungs pa'i 'dab mar rgyal ba'i snang brnyan 'bum gyis sbung pa'i ngo mtshar gyis bkra bas na sku 'bum zhes mtshan du grags shing /
de yang rje bla ma tsong kha pa chen po de nyid sngon bram ze'i khye'ur gyur pa'i dus su 'dren pa mnyam med shAkya'i rgyal bo la shel dkar po dri ma med pa'i phreng ba brgya rtsa zhig phul nas zab mo stong pa nyid kyi lta ba dang 'brel ba'i rdo rje theg pa'i lam rgyas par byed pa'i smon lam btab pa la brten nas mdo smad tsong kha'i yul du yab klu 'bum dge dang yum shing sa a chos kyi sras su sku bltams nas chos rje don grub rin chen ba'i drung du bzhugs te byams pa'i gzhung mdo sde rgyan dang gsang sngags kyi dbang lung du ma zhig /
zhus nas bsnyen sgrub bdag 'jug sogs la shin tu 'grus bar mdzad /

yi dam sangs rgyas byang sems mang pos rjes su bzungs nas byin gyis brlabs /

lo de ka'i sa mo glang lor 'brog ri bo che dga' ldan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling zhes pa'i dgon pa legs par btab ste nub dza lan+d+ha ra nas shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i pha mtha' tshun gyi yul ljongs thams cad du dge 'dun gyi sde rnam par dag pas khyab bang mdzad pa sogs rnam 'dren bu ram shing pa'i rgyal tshab chen po de nyid 'khrungs pa'i yul sku 'bum zhes pa 'di nyid kyi sar 'dus pa'i sde chen por 'phel zhing dbyig 'dzin dang rin chen gnyis pa'i mchod sdong du sri zhu sogs rgyas par rgyal dbang mchog gis stsal ba'i dkar chag tu gsal ba ltar yin la /

skabs gsum dpung sgra dir dir sgrog /
phyi rol bstan pa bud med tshogs / /
glu snyan len cing bshu sgra dir / /
mdun na 'dzin king bzhi bcu gnyis / /
mtshon zhags 'jigs dgrar 'debs la rngams / /
phyi na gtum pa'i btsan 'khor stong / /
btsan gyi 'jigs skad bshu sgra dir / /
mdun bsus kha gdangs lcags spyang dgu / /
dam nyams srog la 'dur zhing rgyug /
rgyab nas zangs kyi 'bar dgu rgyug /
bstan dgra'i bla brku'i las la brtson / /
bsrung ma 'khor tshogs rgya mchor bcas / /
rab tu dang bas 'dud cing bstod / /
gsang sngags bdag po chen po dang / /
grub dbang padma thod phreng gis / /
bka' bsgos dam tshig legs gtad de / /
dbang gis yongs smin gsang mtshan gsol / /
gsang sngags bstan pa bsrung bar bskos / /
rgyal bstan srung mdzad bstod par bgyi / /
sngon gyi dam tshig g.yel med par / /
sha khrag gtor tshogs 'di bzhes la / /
rnal 'byor sgrub po'i bsam pa'i don / /
ji ltar bcol ba'i 'phrin las dang / /
yengs med las bcol 'phrin las sgrubs / /
yul phyogs rnams su dmag 'khrug lo nyes dang / /
nad yams dal yams nyer 'tshe kun zhi zhing / /
bsam don gegs med lhun gyis grub pa dang / /

rgyal sras klu dbang mchog la gsol ba 'debs / /
ye shes lus can rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs / /
dur smrig gar gyis rnam rol tsong kha ba'i / /
bstan pa 'dzin skyong spel la rab brtson pa'i / /
grags pa'i mtshan can zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
de ltar snying nas gsol ba btab pa'i mthus / /
rje btsun bla ma srid mthar zhabs brtan cing / /
rje btsun chos kyi rgyal bo cong kha ba'i / /
bstan pa yun du gnas pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces rgyal sras blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho'i skyes rabs don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te bdag gi mkhan po rin po che gong ma lnga pa chen bos mdzad ba'i go rims dang mthun pa ltar 'khrungs rabs brtan bzhugs dang bcas pa 'di ni zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis bskul ngo dang bstun chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa dge zhing bkra shis par gyur cig /
! swasti /
'di ltar bdag gi 'bad bas bsgrubs pa yi / /
dge ba'i rtsa ba ji snyed mchis pa des / /
'di nas skye ba gzhan gyis mchod bar / /
rnam smin brgyad ldan rten bzang thob par shog /
de tshe jo bo yab sras sku mched gsum / /
'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa'i / /
thun mong min pa'i rnam thar gtsang ma la / /
dang cing mos pa'i sems kyis 'jug par shog /
khyad par rgyal ba yab sras rnam gsum gyis / /
'bral ba med par dgyes bzhin rjes bzungs te / /
dad brtson shes rab phul du byung ba dang / /
dam chos bdud rtsi'i dpal la spyod par shog /
de yi mthu las gsung rab kun gyi gnad / /
skyes bu gsum gyi lam gyi rim pa yis / /
rang rgyud sbyong zhing phyin drug bsdu bzhi yis / /
'gro kun don du sangs rgyas myur thob shog /
gnas skabs su yang rigs rgyud mnga' thang dang / /
tshe bsod 'dod dgu'i dpal 'byor sna tshogs ba / /
dge ldan bstan pa rgyas @# / /
phyir 'phel ba dang / /
'dzam gling bde legs chen bos khyab par shog /
ces ba 'di ni rgyal mo tshe ring bkra shis yum sras kyi 'bad ba chen bos byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i lung gsan ba'i dge rtsa rdzogs byang du bsngo ba'i phyir du chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa dge legs 'phel / /
! oM swasti /
rgyal kun yum gcig ston ka'i zla ltar dkar / /
zhal gcig phyag g.yon ut+pal sngon pos mdzes / /
'gro la tshe dang ye shes stsol mdzad pa'i / /
rje btsun yid bzhin 'khor lo'i zhabs la 'dud /
ces ba 'di ni rgyal sras sUr+ya'i zhal 'don du chos smra ba'i btsun ba blo bzang ye shes kyis smras ba dge legs 'phel / /
! na mo many+dzu g+ho ShA ya /
dus gsum rgyal ba'i yab gcig 'jam ba'i dbyangs / /
rgya bod kun tu sbrul ba'i zlos gar gyis / /
bstan ba'i snying po gsal bar mdzad pa yi / /
blo bzang grags ba'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
mgon po gang de'i thugs rje'i byin rlabs kyis / /
blo bzang bstan ba'i nyi ma chos kyi rje / /
gdul bya padmo'i gnyen du 'byon ba dang / /
bzhed don ma lus lhun gyis 'grub par shog /
bdag kyang deng nas tshe rabs thams cad du / /
rdo rje 'chang dbang blo bzang grags ba dang / /
bshes gnyen dam bas 'bral med rjes 'dzin cing / /
theg mchog chos kyi dpal la sbyod bar shog /
skye zhing skye ba dag ni thams cad du / /
dal 'byor rten thob bstan la rab byung nas / /
thos bsam sgom dang 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la / /
blo gros spobs pa'i snang ba thob par shog /
de ltar sgrub la gnas gsum mkha' 'gro dang / /
chos skyong bsrung mas rtag tu grogs mdzad nas / /
rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'dzin skyong spel ba la / /
bar gcod bgegs kyi mtshan ma zhi bar shong / /
ces ba 'di ni dbon chung blo bzang rgyal mtshan gyis bskul pa'i ngor chos smra ba'i btsun ba blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
blo bzang bstan pa'i kun+da'i tshal yangs por / /

'dzin la zla med lha mi'i skyabs gcig bu / /
tshogs gnyis ye shes yon tan yongs rdzogs pa'i / /

! oM bde legs su gyung cig /

bkra shis / /
! swasti /
blo bzang mkhyen pa'i dkyil 'khor rab rgyas shing / /
ye shes 'phrin las 'od stong 'bar ba yis / /
dad ldan padmo'i tshal rab kha 'byed ba'i / /

bslu med bla ma yi dam byin rlabs dang / /

phyogs bcu'i zhing bzhugs rgyal ba kun gyi / /

shugs drag dad pas gsol ba 'debs so / /

ces pa 'di ni nang so lcang lo can tshe brtan mgon po pha bus 'di lta bu zhig dgos zhes bskul ba la brten chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o /
dge legs 'phel / /
! na mo gu ru /
'dir bla ma'i rnal 'byor sgom par 'dod pas /
thog mar bla ma bsten pa'i phan yon ma bsten pa'i nyes dmigs rnams zhib tu bsam zhing /
khyad par dam tshig dang sdom pa tshul bzhin mi bsrung ba rnams kyis sangs rgyas byang sems rnams la mchod kyang dgyes bzhin bzhes pa'i dge ba mi thob mod /
'on kyang de lta bu'i slob mas bla ma so so skye bo zhig la mchod pa'ang /
sangs rgyas byang sems rnams byon nas bla ma de'i lus la bzhugs shing /
mchod pa rnams dgyes bzhin bzhes pa dang /
phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad mchod pa las bla ma'i ba sbu'i bu ga gcig mchod pa phan yon che ba'i tshul la nges pa drangs nas /
dad pa chen po'i ngang nas /
rang 'jigs byed lta bu'i nga rgyal la gnas bzhin pas /
'bru gsum lan gsum brjod pas /
nang mchod mchod rdzas rnams byin gyis brlabs la /
'di ltar /
mdun gyi nam mkhar dpag bsam ljon pa'i rtser / /
seng khri pang za nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor steng / /
rtsa ba'i bla ma gsum ldan rdo rje 'dzin / /
phyag g.yas chos 'chad g.yon ba glegs bam bsnams / /
mtha' skor rim bzhin dngos rgyud bla ma dang / /
yi dam sangs rgyas byang sems nyan rang dang / /
dpa' bo dpa' mo mkha' 'gro chos skyong dang dam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyis bskor bar gyur / /
gnas gsum rdo rje gsum gyi sa bon gyis / /
legs par mtshan zhing hUM yig 'od zed gyis / /
rang bzhin gnas nas so so'i ye shes pa / /
spyan drangs dam tshig pa dang dbyer med gyur / /
gang gi zhabs sen gus pas brten pa yis / /
sku gsum go 'phang myur du stsol mdzad cing / /
gnas skabs bsam don yid bzhin 'grub pa yi / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo / /
dngos bshams yid sprul phyi nang gsang ba yi / /
mchod tshogs kun 'bul sdig ltung so sor bshags / /
rang gzhan dge la rjes su yi rangs shing / /
chos 'khor bskor phying bskal brgyar bzhugs su gsol / /
de ltar tshogs bsags spel dang bshags pa yi / /
dge ba'i rtsa ba ji snyed mchis pa dang / /
khyad par bshes gnyen tshul bzhin bsten pa yi / /
dge ba rdzogs ba'i byang chub phyir bsngo'o / /
gang gi rnam dpyod thugs rje'i 'khor lo yis / /
dge legs rgya mtsho'i dpal la dbang bsgyur zhing / /
gdul bya thar ba'i gling du 'khrid mdzad pa'i / /
drin can bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
rnam dag nges 'byung shing rta la brten nas / /
bslab gsum rim gnyis gdams pa dbang gi rgyal / /
mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i klong nas 'dren mdzad ba'i / /
thar 'dod deng dpon mchog la gsol ba 'debs / /
dge legs rgya mtsho'i dpal gyis bskrun pa yi / /
mang thos tshul ldan 'khor lo bzhi dang ldan / /
don gyi snying bo thar lam ston pa yi / /
mtshan @# / /
mchog don dang ldan la gsol ba 'debs / /
bslu med dkon mchog yi dam dpa' bo dang / /
mkha' 'gro chos skyong bsrung ma'i mthu stobs kyis / /
rgyal ba'i bstan 'dzin dge legs rgya mtsho'i dpal / /
zhabs pad bskal brgya'i bar du brtan par shog /
de nas /
skyabs gsum kun 'dus kyi ngo bo bla ma rin po che la gsol ba 'debs so / /
bdag gi blo chos su 'gro bar byin gyis brlab tu gsol / /
chos lam du longs bar byin gyis brlab tu gsol / /
khyad par skyes bu gsum gyi lam gyi rim pa'i rtogs pa khyad par can myur du rgyud la skye bar byin gyis brlab tu gsol /
zhes gdung shugs drag pas gsol ba btab pas /
bla ma'i sku las bdud rtsi sna lnga 'od zer dang bcas pa'i rgyun byung ba /
rang gi lus sems la zhugs pas /
rang rgyud la bla ma'i byin rlabs zhugs par bsam mo / /
de nas /
de ltar mchod cing gsol ba btab pa'i mthus / /
deng nas skye zhing skye ba thams cad du / /
bshes gnyen dam pas 'bral med rjes 'dzin cing / /
bsam sbyor gnyis kyis tshul bzhin bsten par shog /
de nas de yis ji ltar gdams pa bzhin / /
dal 'byor don che rnyed bar dka' ba dang / /
nam 'chi nges med ngan 'gro'i 'jigs pa yis / /
dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro bar shog /
skye rga na 'chi nges med ngoms mi shes / /
'du byed sdug bsngal phra mo'i tshul rtogs nas / /
bslab gsum nyams len gnad la brtson pa yis / /
rnam grol thar pa'i gling du bgrod par shog /
rang nyid ji bzhin drin can pha ma rnams / /
sdug bsngal gsum gyis mnar ba'i tshul bsams nas / /
byams dang snying rje byang chub sems bskyed nas / /
phyin drug bsdu ba bzhi la spyod par shog /
thun mong lam sbyangs rnam dag dbang bzhi thob / /
dam tshig sdom ba srog ltar gces 'dzin cing / /

tshe gcig sangs rgyas 'grub pa'i skal ldan shog /
ces se ra rtse'i bla ma dge legs rgya mtsho la gsol ba 'debs tshul /
brtan bzhugs /
lam gyi rim pa la brten pa'i smon lam dang bcas pa zhig dgos zhes sgrub sde phan tshun gyi dge slong ri khrod pa rnams kyis bskul ba'i dor chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa dge legs 'phel / / /
! oM swasti /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor sgom par 'dod pas skyabs 'gro sems bskyed tshad med bzhi sgom pa sngon du btang /
bla ma bsten pa'i phan yon /
ma bsten pa'i nyes dmigs rnams bsam zhing /
dge sems khyad par can gyi ngang nas 'di ltar gdon par bya ste /

chu skyes nyi zla rgyas pa'i dkyil 'khor steng / /

zhal gcig phyag gnyis phyag g.yas chos 'chad dang / /

chos gos gsum gsol gser mdog paN zhwas mdzes / /

dpa' bo mkha' 'gro bsrung mas bskor bar gyur / /
rigs kun bdag po @# / /
khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / /
dur smrig gar gyis rnam rol tsong kha pa'i / /
bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan phyogs bcur bsgreng mdzad pa'i / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo / /
phyi nang gsang ba sgrub pa'i mchod pas mchod / /
lus ngag yid kyi sdig ltung thams cad bshags / /
dge la yi rang chos 'khor bskor ba dang / /
bskal brgyar bzhugs gsol dge tshogs byang chub bsngo / /
dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyis ma thul ba'i / /
bdag sogs 'gro ba'i skyabs gyur dge ba'i bshes / /
bka' drin chen po rjes su legs dran pas / /
rtse gcig dang ba'i yid kyis gsol ba 'debs / /
de ltar dang ba'i yid kyis gsol btab pas / /

'bad rtsol med bar lhun gyis grub pa dang / /

! swasti /
'jig rten dbang phyug pad dkar 'chang ba yis / /

bzhengs pa'i dge tshogs zla shel ltar dkar dang / /
tshe rabs sngon nas nyer bsags legs byas dang / /
bstan srungs chos skyong rgya mtsho'i mthu stobs kyis / /

zab gsal rno myur yangs pa'i rnam dpyod kyis / /

rlabs chen rgyal sras spyod pa mthar phyin te / /
ma rnams don du sangs rgyas myur thob shog /

! oM bde legs su gyur cig /

lan gsum mam /

mjug tu /

! oM swasti /
rgyal ba gnyis pa blo bzang grags pa yi / /
mdo sngags chos kyi de nyid kun la mkhas / /
rig grol 'dus pa'i dbus na mngon mtho ba / /
yongs 'dzin dam pa'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /

gtso / /

oM tsa ren+d+rA ya bdag cag dpon slob 'khor dang bcas pa'i phyi nang gi bar du gcod pa thams cad zhi ba dang /
dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rgyas par mdzod swA hA / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
lha mi'i ston pa mnyam med shAkya'i tog /
bka' gdams bstan pa'i srol btod mar me mdzad / /
yab sras rgyal ba gnyis pa tsong kha pa / /
rgyud bar bcas la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo / /
de la 'dir sde chen sgrub sde dang /
dge ldan gsang sngags lung du bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun rnams kyi bca' khrims spyi sgos kyi spang blang bya tshul la /
dgon phan tshun gyi mtho khongs tshun chad du gnas brtan la gnang ba ma zhus par mi nag dang bud med kyi rigs mi gtong zhing bud med skya ser gang yang zhag sdod mi byed /
thag rings dang spyi @# / /
don du 'ongs pa sogs mi nag skyes pa mi sdod dka' med byung nam gtogs nye skor ba rnams kyang zhag tu mi sdod /
bud med kyi rigs bla brang dang spyi khang du 'gro dgos byung na ma gtogs gzhan spyil bu so sor mi gtong /
tshul khrims dag pa shin tu gal che bas gzhi gsum gyi lag len rgyun gnas dang /
lo re'i nang du dbyar dgun ston dpyid bzhi la mtshams grwa zla ba re 'chag med byed /
mtshams dus spyi don dang dmigs bsal rkyen dgos byung na ma gtogs gnang ba mi zhu /
rgyun bar yang gnang ba ma zhus par grong khyim sogs su mi 'gro /
gnang ba thob kyang spyi don dang chos zhu ba la sogs dmigs bsal bab 'brel yod nam a gtogs zhag bcu las lhag pa mi sdod /
gal te sdod na zhag grangs kyi phyogs spyi sor 'bul zhing /
zla ba 'das na phogs steng du sgrub sde so sor nyin gang zhabs tog dang /
lo 'das na sgrub grwar mi 'jug /
sgrub grwar 'jug mtshams phogs dus yin pas chu ma 'phrod pa sogs dge sbyor mi 'phel ba'i dmigs bsal bkra shis lhun por dgongs khrol zhus grags rnams phogs lhag spyi sor 'bul /
zla re'i nang du gso sbyongs gnyis dang /
dgu gtor sgrub mchod gnyis la 'du 'tshog dang /
de phyin mchod yon yab sras rnams kyi zhabs brtan gus sgrub dmigs bsal byung nas gtogs ja thug spyil bu so sor 'bul zhing /
so so nas bag yengs spangs te blo nus dang bstun pa'i bsnyen sgrub dang mdo sngags gnyis kyi lam gyi lam gyi rim par nyams 'khrid la brtson par byed /
bsam gtan gyi tsher ma sgra yin pas gling gser tu rgyang 'bod mi byed /
chos mthun 'tsho sgrub ma gtogs dgos med khe tshong sogs dge sbyor la gnod pa'i yo lang mi byed /
dus bde min ci byung yang gzhan gyi bskyas khungs mi byed /
bstan don spyi rim sogs dmigs bsal byung na ma gtogs gzhan don du ming btags pa'i grong chog gi rigs gtan nas mi byed /
'dir ma 'khod pa'i dus dang bstun pa'i sgrigs lam kun spyod spang blang skabs babs thams cad kyang bla ma'i ngag bkod ltar byed cing /
bag yod pa'i sgo nas spyir thar pa don gnyer dang /
'di dag gi rgyab rten du paN chen thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i re khrod pa'i bca' yig yang yang bltas nas dran pa gso zhing /
mdor na lto gos gtam gsum don du gnyer ba'i tshe 'di'i snang shas dang /
skye ba gzhan du lha mi'i bde ba thob 'dod kyi phyi ma'i snang shas bzlog pa'i gnyen por dal 'byor don che rnyed dka' /
'chi ba mi rtag ba /
las rgyu 'bras rnams rgyud dang 'dres nges pa bskyangs nas /
blo chos su 'gro ba dang /
chos lam du 'gro ba'i thabs su lam rim blo sbyong sogs la zhib tu bltas nas thar pa'i grong khyer du 'jug par 'tshal lo / /
gtsug lag khang rnams klog pa dang / /
kha ton gyis rgyas legs gnas sho /
rtag par dge 'dun mthun pa dang / /
dge 'dun don yang 'grub par shog /

phun sum ldan pa thob par shog /

! oM bde legs su gyur cig /

swasti /
rab 'byor rigs ldan slob dpon legs ldan 'byed / /
a b+h+yA 'gos lo sa skya paN+Di / /
g.yung ston mkhas grub bsod nams phyogs glang dang / /

blo bzang ye shes skyes rabs snang brnyan 'di / /
'tsho byed dge slong nam mkha' don grub kyis / /
dad pas kun bslangs 'bad pas bsgrub pa'i mthus / /

bzhed don tshul bzhin sgrub la skyo ngal med / /
gso rig mdo sngags yon tan mthar phyin te / /
'gro kun nyon mongs nad las sgrol bar shog /

! gang zhig 'chi ba'i tshe na sems dang bas / /

bde ba can du skye bar zhal ba zhes pa'i / /

! sngon tshe spyad pa spyod tshe smon lam gyis / /

! gser gyi lhun po las kyang rab brjid cing / /

! sngon gyi smon lam rgyas pa'i khyad par gyis / /

mya ngan med mchog zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo / /

pas kyang / /

! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
'dir 'od dpag med la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor sgom par 'dod pas /
skyabs 'gro sems bskyed tshad med bzhi sgom pa sngon du btang /
mdun gyi nam mkhar rma byas bteg pa'i rin po che'i khri'i steng du padma dang zla ba'i gdan la drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma dang dbyer mi phyed pa'i bcom ldan 'das mgon po 'od dpag med sku mdog byu ru'i lhun po la nyi ma bye ba'i mdangs kyis 'khyud ba ltar dmar zhing 'od zer 'phro ba /
zhi zhing 'dzum pa'i nyams ldan zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa dgu gtsug tor dang ldan cing /

sku la chos gol dmar po gsum gsol zhing /

de'i g.yas su byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs sku mdog dkar po phyag g.yas padma dkar po 'dzin pa /
g.yon du byang chub sems dpa' mthu chen thob g.yon padma'i yul 'dzin pa'i steng na rdo rje mtshan pa gnyis kAng gtso bo la phyogs pa'i tshul gyis byang chub kyi shing dpag tshad stod phrag drug cu pa'i mdun na bzhugs pa /
de dag gi g.yas g.yon du nye ba'i sras gzhan rnams dang sprul pa'i nyan thos mang po rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkha' la 'phur ra sogs rtse zhing bzhugs pa /

mngon par 'tshang rgya de la phyag 'tshal lo / /
byang chub brnyes nas chos 'khor bskor ba'i tshe / /
'dus pa gsum rer dung phyur phrag dgu dang / /
bye ba drug bzhi gnyis kyi dgra bcom gyi / /
'khor gyis yongs su bskor la phyag 'tshal lo / /
zhing 'di'i dngos kyi gdul bya rdzogs pa na / /
zag med mya ngan 'das pa'i dbyings bzhugs nas / /
sku gdung ril po gcig tu bzhugs pa sogs /
tha ma'i mdzad pa bstan la phyag 'tshal lo / /
bde gshegs snga ma'i gdul bya le lo can / /
phal cher byams pa'i bstan la bya ba byed / /
dam bca'i gzungs thos ri dwags bya rnams kyang / /
ma 'ongs rdzogs byang lung bstan 'thob par gsungs / /
! bris sku mthong ba don ldan cho 'phrul dang / /
sman bla'i zhing bkod byams pa'i mdzad pa bcu / /
'jam dbyangs rnam 'phrul sman bla yab sras kyi / /
ring lugs skyong la ngang tshul bzang po can / /
sngon byon mkhas pa'i tshogs la 'gran bzod pa'i / /
pir thogs dbang po rje drung mkhos khang pa / /
blo bzang nor bu mched grogs slob 'khor gyis / /
dang mdun gus pas bsgrims te gzabs nas bris / /
'di ltar bsgrubs las byung ba'i rnam dkar dge /
kun+da dung ltar dkar ba ji snyed par / /
mar gyur 'gro ba kun la phan don du / /
bla med rdzogs byang chen por bsngo bar bgyi / /
bkra shis / /
! bris sku mthong ba don ldan la /
na mo gu ru many+dzu g+ho ShA ya /
gdengs can dbang pos bzungs pa'i 'dab brgya'i steng / /
gser ri ltar brjid shAkya'i rgyal po ni / /
'khor dang bcas pa'i ras bris mthong tsam gyis / /
mi dge bcu dang mtshams med nye ba lnga / /
sdig kun byang zhing tshogs gnyis yongs su rdzogs / /
gtsang gnas 'phags pa'i gnas su skye 'gyur zhes / /
'jam dpal rtsa ba'i rtog par gsungs pa la / /
snying nas yid ches dad pas dpa' ba dang / /
phyag dang mchod pa nyin mtshan nyid byed cing / /
sdig ltung @# / /
kun bshags slan chad mi bgyid sdom / /
rjes su yi rang chos 'khor bskor ba sogs / /
bsag sbyang gnad la brtson pa lhod med rigs / /
bkra shis / /
! na mo shAkya mu na ye /
thub dbang 'od ma'i tshal du bzhugs pa'i tshe / /
mu stegs ston pa drug gi phrag dog gis / /
gzugs can snying por go'u ta ma dang / /
rdzu 'phrul 'gran zhes bskul tshe spyos te btang / /
slar yang mnyan yod grong khyer chen po ru / /
yang yang 'gran zhes gsal rgyal rgyal por bskul / /
de yis ston par zhugs te 'gran no zhes / /
bde bar gshegs pas 'gran zhes zhal gyis bzhes / /
de nas dpyid ra'i dga' ba dang po la / /
gsal rgyal gyis mchod tshems shing btsugs ma thag /
sdong po lo 'dab 'bras bus rab brjid pa'i / /
dpag bsam dbang po skad cig de la byung / /
bzang po dang por u tra ya nas mchod / /
g.yas g.yon rin che sa 'dzin chen po 'khrungs / /
shun tsis mchod tshe zhal bsil bor ma thag /
yan lag brgyad ldan chu klung chen por gyur / /
de nas nyin gsum mchod sprin spros pa'i tshe / /
de snyed ngo mtshar cho 'phrul du ma bstan / /
dga' ba gnyis pa bzang po gnyis pa la / /
mchod tshe 'khor rnams phan tshun sems shes shing / /
'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po chen por gyur / /
tshes brgyad seng ge'i khri las srin po dang / /
rdo rje 'dzin pas cham rngams drag po yis / /
ston pa drug bcom dgu khri srid las bsgral / /
de nas rang byung snang ba brgyad pa dang / /
'jig rten skyong dang mgon med zas sbyin gyis / /
mchod tshe sku yi bkod pa rgya che zhing / /
gsung gi cho 'phrul du ma rim par bstan / /
bcu gnyis bdag po'i tshes dang bcu gsum dang / /
bcu bzhi rgyal ba'i sku mchog dam pa dang / /
shing rta stong dang nyis brgya lnga bcus gang / /
yar ngo'i nya yi tshes pa bzang po la / /
phyag sor las byung gser sbyangs 'od zer gyis / /
las 'bras mngon sum bstan nas ston pa drug /
mtho ris thar pa'i lam la 'dren par mdzad / /
de ltar rgyal ba'i dus chen bzhi po la / /
dge ba'i rtsa ba ji snyed bgyis pa rnams / /
sa ya phrag brgya'i 'gyur du rgyal bas gsungs / /
de yang zhib mor rtsis na de yi tshe / /
nas phul gang zhig lhag bsam rnam dag gis / /
gzhan la sbyin par btang na nas phul ni / /
sa ya phrag brgya ra sbyin par 'gyur ba'i phyir / /
nas khal 'bum phrag brgyad dang sum khri dang / /
sum stong sum brgya sum cu rtsa gsum dang / /
bre drug phul bzhi sbyin pa'i 'bras bu 'byung / /
de ltar gsungs la yid ches skyes nas ni / /
dus chen rnams la dge la 'bad par mdzod / /
bkra shis / /
! blo gros bzang po'i kun gsal rab yangs par / /
tshogs gnyis dpal gyi dkyil 'khor rab tu rdzogs / /
ye shes 'od stong phyogs brgyar 'phro ba yis / /
gdul bya'i ku mud 'byed la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo ldan grang med gdul byar bzang po'i lam / /
tshul @# / /
bzhin ston la ye shes spyan ldan zhing / /
snyigs dus 'gro ba'i skyabs gcig dam pa mchog /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
smon 'jug blo yi rtsa ba rab tu brtan / /
bzang po'i spyod pa'i yal 'dab stong ldan zhing / /
ye shes 'bras bu smin pa'i khur gyis brjid / /
bshes gnyen dpag bsam dbang por gsol ba 'debs / /
blo chen rgyal sras bzang po'i spyod pa rnams / /
gcig tu bsdus nas tshul bzhin 'doms pa la / /
ye shes sems dpa'i tshogs dang dbyer med pa'i / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
de ltar snying nas gsol ba btab pa'i mthus / /
bdag sogs deng nas tshe rabs thams cad du / /
rje btsun bla mas 'bral med rjes bzungs te / /
rnam smin brgyad ldan rten bzang myur thob shog /
de nas thun mong lam gyis rgyud sbyangs shing / /
bla med rdo rje theg par rab zhugs te / /

! swasti /
bde gshegs gtsug tor las 'khrungs gdugs dkar can / /
bskal bzang 'dren pa stong gi byin rlabs kyis / /

zhabs zung mi 'gyur yun ring brtan par shog /
dpal mgon sde lnga dmag zor rgyal mo dang / /
rnam mang thos sras 'khor bcas mthu stobs kyis / /
bstan 'dzin dam pa yun ring zhabs brtan cing / /
'phrin las phyogs mthar rgyas pa'i bkra shis shog /

ye shes khyung khra'i 'phrin las gzi byin gyis / /
'phags pa bsod nams lhun grub dge legs dpal / /
steng 'og gdon gyi g.yul las rgyal bar shog /

! na mo gu ru bud+d+ha bo d+hi satwA ya /
ngag dbang rgyal ba gnyis pa tsong kha pa'i / /
snyan rgyud gdams pa bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal / /
gang thugs zab yangs rgya mtshor legs 'khyil ba'i / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
sngon nas sngon du legs par goms pa yi / /
bzang po'i bag chags sad pa'i snying stobs can / /
dka' dpyad drag pos gdams pa nyams bzhes pa'i / /
ngag dbang bsam 'phel zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
srid pa'i phun tshogs snying po med gzigs nas / /
tshe 'di'i rnam g.yeng bya ba ring spangs te / /
gdams pa'i snying po rang gis nyams bzhes nas / /
gzhan la legs par 'doms la gsol ba 'debs / /

drang srong bden tshig grub pa'i smon lam dang / /
chos skyong bsrung @# / /
ma 'khor bcas mthu stobs kyis / /
bshes gnyen dam pa yun ring zhabs brtan shog /

bshes gnyen dam pas dgyes bzhin rjes bzungs te / /
skyes bu gsum gyi lam gyi rim pa dang / /

dge slong blo bzang rgyal mtshan /
dge slong ngag dbang dpal ldan /

! swasti /
rje btsun sgrol ma bsgrub par 'dod pas /
skyabs 'gro sems bskyed tshad med bzhi sngon du btang /
de nas oM swA b+hA wa shud+d+ha sarbad+har+m+ma swa b+hA wa shud+d+hony+haM /
stong pa nyid du gyur /
stong pa'i ngang las paM las padma dang a las zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng du rang gi sems nyid tAM yig dkar po las 'od 'phros /
sems can thams cad kyi mi shes pa'i mun pa dang tshe'i bar gcod thams cad bsal / /
rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa la mnyes pa'i mchod pa phul /
tshur 'dus yongs su gyur pa las /
rang nyid jo mo sgrol ma yid bzhin 'khor lo ston zla ltar dwangs pa zhi zhing 'dzum pa'i nyams can zhal gcig phyag gnyis spyan gsum ma /
phyag zhabs kyi mthil na rnam thar sgo bzhi mtshon pa'i spyan re re mnga' ba /
g.yas mchog sbyin g.yon udpa la'i sdong bu'i rtsa ba thugs kar mtheb srin gyis bzungs pa'i yal ga gyes pa'i dbus ma kha shag ste bye ba /
g.yas 'dab ma spud nas 'bras bu yod pa /
g.yon pa kha ma bye bas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas mtshon pa /
dbu skra ral pa phyed spyi bor bcings shing phyed gsil bur grol ba /
dbu'i gtsug tu nyi zla'i mdangs 'phrog pa lta bu'i nor bus brgyan pa /
gzhan yang dbu rgyan snyan rgyan mgul rgyan la sogs pas spras shing dar sna tshogs pa'i na bza' can zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la sku rgyab drang por brten pa /
zhabs gnyis rdo rje'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'i spyi bor oM dkar po /
mgrin par AH dmar po /
thugs kar tAM yig dkar po hUM sngon pos mtshan pa /
thugs ka'i hUM las 'od 'phros /
bde ba can sogs rang bzhin gyi gnas rnams nas ye shes pa spyan drangs /
dam tshig pa dang gnyis su med par gyur /
slar yang thugs ka'i hUM las 'od zer 'phros /
dbang gi lha rnams spyan drangs /
khyed rnams kyis bdag la mngon par dbang bskur du gsol /
zhes gsol ba btab pas de rnams kyis ye shes kyi bdud rtsis gang ba'i bum pa thogs nas oM sarba ta thA ga ta a b+hiShe ka ta sa ma ya shri ye AHhUM /

swA hA'i bar gyis mchod pa 'bul /
'od dpag med mgon thugs rje'i 'od zer las / /
legs 'khrungs 'gro ba'i gdung skyob rgyal ba'i yum / /

yan lag mchog gi gtsug gis phyag 'tshal lo /
zhes pas bstod /
thugs kar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng du 'khor lo dkar po rtsib sa brgyad pa mu khyud gsum dang bcas pa'i lte bar tAM yig dkar po /
de'i mdun du oM /
mdun nas brtsam te rtsibs brgyad la tA re tut+tA re swa' rnams 'god cing /
tAM yig gi rgyab tu 'god /
mu khyud dang po A li g.yon skor dang /
gnyis pa la kA li g.yas skor / /
gsum pa la rten 'brel snying pos bskor ba las 'od zer dkar po'i tshogs 'phros /
zhi ba'i las 'grub par byas 'od zer ba spu'i sgo nas phyir 'phros /
rang gi mtha' skor du 'od zer dkar po'i gur khyim gyis bskor /
yang sngags 'phreng rnams las 'od zer ser po'i tshogs 'phros /
rgyas ba'i las 'grub par byas /
'od zer dkar po'i gur khyim gyi mthar 'od zer ser po'i gur khyim gyis bskor /
yang 'od zer dmar po'i tshogs 'phrogs dbang gi las rnams 'grub par byas /
'od zer ser po'i mtha' skor du 'khod /
yang 'od zer nag po'i tshogs 'phros /
drag po'i las 'grub par byas /
'od zer ljang khu'i tshogs 'phros /
las rab 'byams 'grub par byas /
'od zer mchin kha'i tshogs 'phros /
de rnams brtan par byas /
'dod zer ljang khu'i gur khyim gyis bskor bar bsams nas yi ge bcu pa'i bzlas pa gang 'grub byas te /
yi ge brgya pas lhag chad kha bskang zhing brtan par byas /
dge pa 'di yis myur du bdag /
rje btsun sgrol ma 'grub gyur nas / /
'gro ba gcig kyang ma lus pa / /
de yi sa la 'god par shog /
ces jo bos 'brom ston pa la gsungs pa'i sgrub thabs sras don ma dang mthun par byas pa 'di ni ye shes dge slong gis bskul ba'i ngor chos smra ba'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa dge legs su gyur cig /
! na mo gu ru /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor sgom par 'dod pas /
skyabs 'gro sems bskyed tshad med bzhi bsgom pa sngon du btang /
bla ma bsten pa'i phan yon /
ma bsten pa'i nyes dmigs rnams bsam zhing /
dge sems khyad par can gyi ngang nas 'di ltar gdon par bya ste / /
! mdun gyi lha lam yangs bar seng khri dang / /
chu skyes nyi zla rgyas pa'i dkyil 'khor steng / /
rtsa ba'i bla ma dkar ser 'dzum dkar 'phro / /
zhal gcig phyag gnyis phyag g.yas chos 'chad dang / /

chos gos gsum gsol gser mdog paN zhus mjes / /

dur smrig gar gyis rnam rol tsong kha ba'i / /
bstan pa'i @# / /
rgyal mtshan phyogs bcur sgreng mdzad ba'i / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la phyag tshal lo / /
phyi nang gsang ba sgrub pa'i mchod pas mchod / /
lus ngag yid kyi sdig lhung thams cad bshags / /
dge la yi rab chos 'khor bskor ba dang / /
bskal brgyar bzhugs gsol dge tshogs byang chub bsngo / /
dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyis ma thul ba'i / /
bdag sogs 'gro ba'i skyabs gyur dge pa'i bshes / /
bka' drin chen po rjes su legs dran bas / /
rtse gcig dang ba'i yid kyis gsol pa 'debs / /
de ltang dang ba'i yid kyis gsol btab pas / /
dpal ldan bla mas 'bral med rjes bzungs te / /
nges 'byung byang sems yang dag lta pa la / /

'bad rtsol med par lhun gyis grub pa dang / /
bshad sgrub bstan pa dar ba'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di ni sngags ram pa bkra shis rgyas tshogs bskul ba'i ngor chos smra ba'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis smras ba dge zhing bkra shis par gyur cig /
! sra sti /
'dul ba lung rnams la thun mong du /
rgyal ba'i bstan pa'i snying po 'dul ba lung / /
bsod nams dpal 'dzom dad pas bzhengs pa'i mthus / /
rgyal bstan spyi dang rgyal pa gnyis pa yi / /
mdo sngags bstan pa dar zhing rgya par shog /
! 'bum po ti bcu brung la thun mong du /
dus gsum rgyal ba ma lus bskyed mdzad ma / /
stong phrag brgya ba'i sher phyin legs bzhengs pas / /
bstan 'dzin spyi dang gangs can 'gro ba'i mgon / /
rgyal ba yab sras bskal brgyar zhabs brtan shog /
! nyi khri rnams la thun mong du /
yum 'bring nyi khri lnga stong bsgrubs pa'i dges / /
phyag rdor sprul pa stong btsan 'gar gyi rigs /
bstan pa'i sbyin bdag dga' ldan skyid shod pa / /
rigs rgyud mnga' thad chab srid brtan par shog /
! khri brgyad stong pa la thun mong du /
khri dang brgyad stong sher phyin yum gyi mdo / /
lhag bsam dag bas bzhengs pa'i rnam dkar gegs / /
bdag dang mar gyur 'gro ba ma lus pa'i / /
sdig sgrib kun byang tshogs gnyis rdzogs par shog /
! shes rab khri ba dang brgyad stong pa gnyis la /
shes rab khri ba bsdus pa brgyad stong pa / /
shog dkar 'dzin ma'i ngos la bkod pa'i mthus / /
chos kun gnas lugs rtogs ba'i shes rab kyis / /
sdug bsngal rtsa ba drungs nas 'byin par shog /
! sna tshogs khri bar /
shar phyin la sogs sna tshogs rgyal ba'i bka' / /
bsod nams dpal 'dzom dang pa sgrub pa'i dges / /
sgo gsum ma dag dri ma kun sbyangs nas / /
ngan song gnas su slar yang mi lhung shog /
! phal chen drug la /
phal chen la sogs rgyal ba'i gsung rab kun / /
bzhengs la mthun pa bsgrub pa'i lus can rnams / /
dal 'byor rten bzang rgyun mar 'thob pa dang / /
rnam kun @# / /
mkhyen pa'i ye shes mchog thob shog /
! dkon brtsegs drug la /
dkon brtsegs la sogs zab dang rgya che ba'i / /
dri med bka' la sri zhu bgyis pa yis / /
dkon mchog gsum dang nam yang mi 'bral zhing / /
rgyal sras spyod la zhum med slob par shog /
! mdo myang 'das gnyis la /
rgyal ba'i mdzad pa kun gyi mchog gyur ba / /
byang phyogs gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir 'gyur ro 'tshal / /
'bri dang klog dang mchod cing bstod pa rnams / /
mi gnas mya ngan 'das ba myur thob shog /
! rgyud sde rnams la thun mong du /
thub pa'i gsung rab kun gyi rtser son pa / /
gsang chen rgyud sde rgya mtsho 'gyur ro 'tshal / /
bzhengs pa'i dge ba zla bstan 'dzin gyis / /
gser ldan dga' ma'i mngal 'khur lci gyur cig /
! rgyud sde rnams la thun mong du /
thub pa'i gsung rab kun gyis rtser son pa / /
'g+sang chen rgyud sde rgya mtsho 'gyur ro 'tshal / /
bzhengs pa'i dge ba zla shel ltar dkar des / /
mdo sngags bstan pa dar pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di yang stag rtse'i yum bsod nams dbal 'dzom gyis dad brtson chen pos rgal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cig bzhengs pa'i dge rtsa rnams rdzogs byang du bsdo ba'i phyir du chos smra ba'i dge slong blau bzang ye shes kyis smras pa dge zhing bkra shis par gyur cig /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig / /
'jam dpal gshin rje'i gshed dang dbyer med du / /
rtse gcig mos pa'i yul gyur rdo rje 'dzin / /
lha bcas 'gro ba'i gtsug rgyan yid bzhin nor / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
bslu med dkon mchog gsum gyis byin rlabs dang / /
dge ldan bstan srungs rgya mtsho'i mthu stobs kyis / /
blo bzang ye shes zhabs sen rdo rje'i khrir / /
g.yo med 'phrin las phyogs bcur rgyas par shog /
sngon nas bzang po'i las kyis yongs 'brel ba'i / /
dad ldan phu nu tshe rabs thams cad du / /
rje btsun bla mas dgyes bzhin rjes bzungs te / /
mthar thug kun mkhyen go 'phang thob par shog /
ces pa 'di ni pa'i sangs srong btsan bstan skyong gis bla ma dang yi dam dbyer med du gsol ba 'debs shing zhabs pad brtan pa dang /
nged rang phu nu gnyis rjes su 'dzin pa'i smon lam bcas 'khyer bde bzhig dngos zhes bskul ba'i der chos smra ba'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa dge legs su gyur cig /
! oM swasti /
sku bzhi'i bdag nyid drin can bla ma dang / /
dbyar med mgon po yid bzhin nor bu la / /
snying nas 'dud do mchog dang thun mong gi / /
dngos grub ma lus myur du stsal du gsol / /
de la 'dir mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i rjes gnang bya bar 'dod pas /
gnas dben zing bkra shis la nyams dga' bar /

sa gzhi 'am / /
maN+Dal dri bzang gis legs par byugs pa la padma dkar @# / /
po 'dab ma bzhi pa lte ba dmar ser gyi dbus su hUM dkar po dang /
padma'i mtha' me ris skor ba bri /
de'i sted many+dzi'am /

gcig bsdus bzang po'i dur smrig gang rol zhing / /
ye shes sgrib bral bde ba'i dpal mnga' ba / /
yongs 'dzin dam pa yun ring zhabs brtan shog /
sdom gsum bang rim mthon po'i ba gam can / /
mtha' bral rim gnyis don rtogs nor gyis phyug /
rtse gcig mnyam gzhag mi g.yo rab brtan pa'i / /
zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang la gsol ba 'debs / /
bslab gsum dag pa'i dge 'dun 'dus pa'i tshogs / /
khrims gtsang dbyar gyi nor bu'i gnas ltar 'phel / /
blo bzang gsung gi ring lugs nyams med par / /
nyin mtshan kun tu ngal med spyod par shog /
dge 'dis mtshon nas skye ba thams cad du / /
dpal ldan bla mas 'bras med rjes bzungs te / /
mdo sngags yon tan ma lus mthar phyin nas / /
kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i go 'phang myur @# / /
thob shog /
blo bzang gsung gi legs bshad ma lus pa / /
phyogs dus kun tu dar zhing rgyas gyur nas / /
thub pa'i ring lugs mtha' dag rab rgyas shing / /
phun tshogs dpal 'byor rgyas pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di ni snye mo rgyal byed mkhan slob 'dus tshogs rnams kyis bskul ba'i ngor shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa'o / /
! bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo / /
ma he rab tu khros pa'i gdan steng du / /
sku mdog dmar po 'jigs su rung ba'i gzugs / /
zhal gcig phyag gnyis phyag g.yon thod pa'i steng / /
g.yas pa yid bzhin nor bus mtshan pa bsnams / /
zhabs gnyis g.yas bskums g.yon brkyangs bzhugs la bstod / /
blo bzang rgyal ba gnyis pa tsong kha pa'i / /
mdo sngags bstan pa tshul bzhin srung ba dang / /
'phrin las tshul bzhin thogs med sgrub mdzad pa'i / /
dam can gshin rje 'khor dang bcas la bstod / /
rnal 'byor bdag cag dgon gnas dge 'dun sde / /
srung skyo ba g.yel med tshul bzhin sgrub pa dang / /
nag phyogs bdud rigs bar gcod tshar bcad de / /
mthun rkyen tshul bzhin 'grub pa'i 'phrin las mdzod / /
ces pa 'di ni rab 'byams pa ngag dbang chos 'phel gyis nan gyis yang yang bskul ba ltar chos smra ba'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa'o / /
! na mo gu ru many+dzu g+ho ShA ya /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor bsgom par 'dod pas /
skyabs 'gro sems skyed tshad med bzhi sngon du btang /
swa b+hA was stong par sbyangs /
stong pa'i dang las /
rang gi mdun du kun bzang mchod sprin dbus / /
gdong lngas legs bteg 'od 'bar ren chen khri / /
'dab stong ge sar nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor steng / /
rigs brgya'i khyab bdag dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang / /
dbyer med mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan kun gyi rje / /
sku mdog shal ltar mdangs gsal dgyes ba'i zhal / /
phyag g.yas chos 'chad g.yon pa mnyam gzhag steng / /
brgyad khri bzhi stong glegs bam gyis mdzes shing / /
'od stong gzhon nu'i mdangs can chos gos gsum / /
gsol zhing gser mdog paN zhwas legs par mdzes / /
skyabs gsum dkon mchog 'dus pa'i bdag nyid can / /
yid 'phrog 'ja' tshon sna lnga'i gur khyim dbus / /
zhabs gnyis rdo rje skyil krung tshul gyis bzhugs / /
gnas gsum rdo rje gsum mtshan hUM yig gi / /
'od kyis ye shes pa rnams sbyan drangs te / /
dbyer med 'gro ba'i bsod nams zhing du bzhugs / /
mtha' yas rgyal ba kun gyi mkhyen brtse rnams / /
gcig bsdus dur smig gar gyis rnam rol ba / /
bstan dang 'gro ba'i dpal gyur thams cad mkhyen / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo / /
yid 'ong mtsho dang rdzing bu padmas brgyan / /
dri zhim tsan+dan dkar dmar snang gsal dang / /
spos chu'i mtsho chen lha mi'i ro brgyar ldan / /
snyan 'jebs dngos bshams yid kyis sprul nas 'bul / /
thog med dus nas sgo gsum nyes ltung rnams / /
bgyis dang bgyid stsal yi rang ci mchis pa / /
bsam pa thag pas dpal ldan @# / /
bla ma yi / /
spyan sngar bshags shing mi bgyid sdom pa nod / /
sngon bsags skye 'phags dge ba'i las rnams la / /
yang dang yang du dga' ba legs skyes nas / /
rlabs chen dge tshogs rgya cher 'phel 'gyur ba'i / /
rnam dkar bsod nams kun la rjes yi rang / /
ma rig dug gsum dri mas sbags pa rnams / /
mkhyen brtse'i chu gter rgya mtshos rab bsal nas / /
rang rang gdul bya'i blo dang 'tsham pa yi / /
zab dang rgya che'i chos 'khor bskor du gsol / /
bstan dang bdag sogs 'gro ba'i dpal nyid du / /
bshes gnyen mchog gi thugs rje'i 'od zer gyis / /
gdul bya'i blo mun ma lus sel mdzad phyir / /
grangs med bskal brgya'i bang du brtan par bzhugs / /
de yi mthu las tshe rabs kun tu bdag /
mtshan nyid ldan pa'i bshes gnyen dam pa yis / /
'bral ba med par rjes su 'dzin pa dang / /
mdo sngags yon tan ma lus rgyas phyir bsngo / /
de nas dmigs pa dang bcas rang gang mos kyi bla ma'i gsol 'debs sam /
mtshan sngags ci mang bzla / /
rgyal ba kun gyis bsngags pa'i rnam grol lam / /
legs par ston mdzad 'dzam gling mkhas pa'i rgyan / /
bstan dang 'gro ba'i yongs 'dzin dge ba'i bshes / /
dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba rnams kyi mkhyen brtse'i gter / /
legs bar 'byed la thogs med blo gros rgyas / /
thub dbang bstan pa spel la zla bral ba / /
skyabs mgon thugs rje'i gter la gsol ba 'debs / /
dam pa'i chos tshul lha lam yangs pa la / /
lung dang rigs pa'i nyin byed stong 'bar ba / /
skye dgu'i legs byas dpal du shar pa yi / /
rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
'jam mgon bstan pa'i lugs bzang 'dab brgya'i tshal / /
legs bshad sbrang rtse zab mo'i bcud chags pa / /
skal bzang bung ba'i tshogs rnams tshim mdzad pa'i / /
skyabs mgon thugs rje can la gsol ba 'debs / /
yon tan kun gyi gzhi gyur sdom brtson ldan / /
mtha' bral stong nyid rnam dpyod yal 'dab rgyas / /
rim gnyis mthar phyin zung 'jug 'bras bus brjid / /
rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gtsol gsol ba 'debs / /
de ltar dad shugs drag pos gsol btab pas / /
bla ma'i yi ge gsum las bdud rtsi'i rgyun / /
rim dang cig car byung nas bdag nyid kyi / /
sgo gsum thims nas sgrib bzhi rnam par dag /
dbang dang sku bzhi thob cing bla ma nyid / /
dgyes shing thim pas rang dang dbyer med gyur / /
skye ba kun tu yang dag bla ma dang /
zhes sogs ba sngo smon shis brjod rnams skabs sbyar bya'o /
zhes bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'di ni khal kha nas sngom brtson dang ldan pa rje btsun sprul pa'i sku blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi bkas bskul ba la brten nas /
shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa'o / /

ba'i dpal / /

mang+ga laM / /

blo bzang rgyal ba gnyis pa'i mdo sngags kyi / /

! swasti /

! na mo shAkya mu na ye /
rtsa rgyud bshad rgyud la sogs rgyud kyi gzhung / /

! rgyal gsung yum don shes rab pha rol phyin / /
legs par bgyis pas mar gyur 'gro kun gyi / /
sgrib gnyis bag chags bcas ba dag gyur nas / /
kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i bstan ba rgyas gyur cig /
! rgyal ba'i gsung rab kun gyi bcud phyung ba / /

! bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab myang 'das che / /

! dkon mchog brtsegs pa glegs bam bzhengs pa'i mthus / /

grangs med dag pa'i zhing du skye bar shog /
! 'dul lung gsung rab glegs bam bskrun pa yis / /

dmag 'khrug nad yams mi mthun zhi bar shog /
! thub pa'i gsung rab mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i tshogs / /
bskrun la mthun rkyen sgrub pa'i 'gro ba yis / /

'gro kun don du sangs rgyas myur thob shog /
! oM swasti /
bslab gsum rnam dag yon tan kun gyi gzhir / /
blo bzang lung rtogs sa brtol yal 'dab rgyas / /
tshogs gnyis ye shes 'bras bus legs mdzes pa'i / /
bstan 'gro'i mgon po bskal brgyar zhabs brtan shog /
rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin chen chu gter las / /

zab rgyas yid bzhin nor bu'i khur khyer ba'i / /

lhar bcas 'gro ba kun gyi skyabs kyi mchog /
byams dang snying rje'i 'od stong 'phro ba yis / /
skye dgu'i rmongs ba'i mun pa sel mdzad pa'i / /

bsod nams phun sum tshogs pa'i gzhal med khar / /

'phrin las bzang bo'i rgyal mtshan cher bsgreng ba'i / /
yongs 'dzin dam pa bskal brgyar g.yo med shog / /
blo bzang mkhyen brtse'i dpal gos sbrang rtsis gtams / /

skal bzang bung ba'i tshogs rnams tshims mdzad pa'i / /

'bebs mkhas skal bzang rgya mtshor gsol ba 'debs / /

padma nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor rgyas pa'i steng / /
rgyal kun ngo bo gsum ldan bla ma mchog /
rnam pa dur smrig 'dzin pa'i dge sbyong tshul / /
sku mdog dkar dmar dgyes pa'i 'dzum zhal can / /
phyag g.yas chos 'chang g.yon pa ting 'dzin gyi / /

'og min bde ba can sogs zhing mchog nas / /

yon tan 'phrin las bcas pa'i byin rlabs zhugs / /
bla ma gnyis pa zhig byon spyi bor thim / /
sgo gsum sku gsung thugs dang dbyer med gyur /
de ltar dmigs pa dang bcas pas gsol ba btab pas rang nyid bla ma rdo rje 'chang du dngos gnas la gyur song snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang gsal snang brtan po'i sgo nas snying khar pad nyi'i steng du hUM yig gi mthar sngags 'phreng gis bskor ba la spro bsdu'i dmigs pa dang ldan pas bla ma'i mtshan sngags bzla zhing /
mjug tu paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i bar do gsol 'debs sogs dang /
chogs zhing rnams rim gyis bsdus nas mthar bla ma rang la bstim /
skye ba kun tu yang dag bla ma dang zhes sogs bsngo ba smon lam bkra shis rgyas bsdus ci rigs pa bya'o / /
zhes 'di bas mtha'i ri khrod pa / /
bkra shis gling pa dge slong spyis / /
yang yang nan cher bskul ba'i ngor / /

yi / /

rten 'brel rgyu las mar gyur 'gro ba'i mgon / /
mi 'gyur rdo rje'i khri la g.yo med shog /
bdag kyang skye zhing skye ba thams cad du / /
dge ba'i bshes dang nam yang mi 'bral zhing / /

mang+glaM / /
! swasti /
shAkya'i ring lugs mkhar 'phags blo gros kyi / /
snang bas gsung rab 'dab brgya'i tshal phye zhing / /

yang dag tshim bar mdzad la gsol ba 'debs /
zhes pa 'di yang ldang chen bla ma shAkya blo gros kyi gsol 'debs su drung ram pa blo bzang tshe ring gis bskul ba ltar btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
! swasti /
sa gsum 'gro ba'i gnyen gcig bla ma mchog /
srid mthar zhabs brtan rten cing 'brel 'byung du / /

ston pa mchog dang skyabs dngos dam pa'i chos / /

! swasti /
blo chen chos kun mngon gzigs stobs bcu pa'i / /

! swasti /
rmad byung blo mchog mtha' bral yangs pa la / /

'bad med lhun grub 'bebs la gsol ba 'debs /

'di ltar /

! swasti /

! phyag chen gsol 'debs kyi mjug tu /

dgos zhes bskul ba ltar bgyis pa'o / /
! lha chen tshangs pa'i gtsug lag khang bzang mdzes rgyan ljon dmar sa zlas yongs sbud rgyal mtshan zung / /

! oM swasti /

! swasti /

! na mo gu ru many+dzo g+ho ShA ya /

rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i khyon la dbang bsgyur zhing / /
zab lam rim gnyis nor gyis legs phyug pa'i / /
yongs 'dzin dge ba'i bshes la gsol ba 'debs /
zhes pa 'di yang sngags grwa zhal snga nas dpal 'byor rgya mtshor brgyud 'debs su bcug chog pa'i gsol 'debs shig dgos zhes yar 'phel gyis bskul ba ltar bgyis pa'o / /
bkra shis / /
! swasti /
thub dbang gnas brtan bcu drug 'khor dang bcas / /
bde gshegs mched brgyad bde ldan zhing bkod dang / /
rab 'byor 'khrungs rabs bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad / /
bris 'bur ngo mtshar rmad byung bskrun pa'i dges / /
rje btsun bla ma sku tshe rab brtan cing / /
bsil ldan ljongs 'dir bde skyid 'phel ba dang / /
khyad par rgyu sbyor bkra shis tshe ring spun / /
bu tsha tshe ring nad med bde ldan zhing / /
spun bu tsha nye tshe 'das pha ma yis / /
bsags pa'i sdig sgrib nyes ltung kun byang nas / /
pha mar gyur pa'i 'gro ba ma lus pa / /
sgrol phyir myur 'tshang rgya ba'i rgyu ru bsngo /
zhes pa 'di ni bkra shis rdzong kha'i gnyer pa bkra shis tshe ring gis bskul ba ltar shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / /
sarba dza ga to / /
! oM swasti /
dben sa chos kyi pho brang 'dus pa'i tshogs / /
dgyes byed btung ba'i yol go rin chen las / /
bsgrubs dge rgyal bstan phyogs bcur rgyas pa dang / /
'gro kun sangs rgyas go 'phang thob phyir bsngo / /
'dis mtshon rten gsum mchod rdzas dngos ci mchis / /
'jigs mdzad dpa' bo dpal mgon sde lnga dang / /
rnam gsum lha mor gtad kyis bdag zungs la / /
rku 'phrog bsam sbyor log kun drag pos sgrol / /
sa ma ya tiSh+Sha / /
zhes pa'ang dben sa chos kyi pho brang gi tshogs khro'i zhal yig tu bgyis pa'o / /
! swasti /
dmigs med thugs rjes bskyod pa'i zlos gar gyis / /
grangs med zhing du sbrul pas rnam rol ba / /
skyabs gsum kun 'dus dpal ldan bla ma la / /
gus pas gsol 'debs 'bral med rjes gzung gsol /
zhes pa 'di yang dad ldan dpon mo rnam rgyal gyis bskul ba ltar shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
mang+ga laM / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig rlabs chen tshogs gnyis yongs rdzogs 'dzin ma'i ltor / /
thugs bskyed sa bon legs 'khrungs dpag bsam ljon / /
gzhan phan dri bsung srid gsum khyab 'phro ba'i / /
rnam 'dren nyi ma'i gnyen la mgos phyag 'tshal / /
bslab gsum rnam dag gsung skyes 'du ba'i gnas / /
nor bu chos 'khor gtsug lag khang mdzes rgyan / /
dar gyi lnga ldi gos bzang las grub pa'i / /
gong pa bar mtshams 'phan chung gis spa ba / /
dka' bcu blo bzang chos @# / /
grags lhag bsam gyis / /
bsgrubs pa 'dis mtshon rnam dkar dge ba'i tshogs / /
ji snyed spyad kun mar gyur 'gro sgrol ched / /
myur du rdzogs byang thob pa'i rgyu ru bsngo / /
go 'phang mchog de ma thob tshe rabs su / /
dal 'byor rten thob bshes gnyen dam pa yis / /
'bral med rjes 'dzin gsung gi bgo skal la / /
nyer spyod tshangs spyod ldan pa nyid gyur cig /
gnas skabs su yang bar gcod bdud rigs dpung / /
nam mkha'i glang po lta bu dag zhi nas / /
bde skyid phun tshogs rta ljang can zer gyis / /
gangs can 'dzin ma'i khyon kun khyab gyur cig /
ces pa 'di ni dka' bcu blo bzang chos grags kyis srad nor bu chos 'khor du lnga ldi phul ba'i dge sngo'i tshigs bcad cig dgos zhes nan gyis bskul ba'i ngor shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
mang+ga laM / /
! oM swasti /
tshogs gnyis yongs rdzogs rnam 'dren shAkya'i tog /
brgyad khri bzhi stong nyon mongs kun sel sman / /
tshul bzhin spyod pa theg gsum dge 'dun bcas / /
skyabs mchog rnam pa gsum la mgos phyag 'tshal / /
pha rol son pa phan tshogs dbang mo yi / /
sgrib sbyong tshogs gnyis yongs su rdzogs slad du / /
phyag chen brgyud rim rgyad sde rnam pa bzhi'i / /
snang brnyan ldebs bris bcas pa legs bsgrubs dge /
dpag med sngon nas da lta'i bar bsags pa'i / /
mi dge sdig pa'i 0279b tshogs kun byang ba dang / /
phun tshogs yon tan kun gyi rgyan ldan pa'i / /
sku gsum go 'phang dam pa thob phyir bsngo /
zhes pa 'di ni rin chen rtse nas lcam bsod nams g.yang 'dzin gyis yum phun tshogs dbang mo'i dgongs rdzogs su lha khang gsar bzhengs mdzad pa'i dge bsngo'i tshigs bcad cig dgos gsung ba ltar shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
bkra shis / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
bdud dpung 'joms mdzad 'jam dpal gshin rje'i gshed / /
bar gcod kun sel gur mgon phyag bzhi pa / /
dge sdig shan 'byed dam can chos kyi rgyal / /
khyad par srid gsum bdag mo 'dod khams ma / /
dregs pa lcam sring gnod sbyin yang dag shes / /
dam can rgya mtsho 'khor bcas khyed rnams la / /
mkha' spyod gtsug lag khang dang dge 'dun sde / /
rten gsum mchod rdzas spyan gzigs ma lus dang / /
khang phran mkho dgu'i yo byad longs spyod rnams / /
gnyer du gtad do bka' srungs rgya mtsho yis / /
dus kun bsrung zhing bskyab dang sba ba dang / /
nyin mtshan rtag tu ma g.yel me la tshe mdzod / /
log pa'i bsam pas 'phrog cing bcom pa dang / /
thabs kyis rku sogs gzhan du 'khyer byed pa'i / /
mi bsrun sdig ldan mi dang mi min rnams / /
mngon spyod las kyi chad pas tshar chod mdzod / /
dgon gnas dge 'dun dkon mchog rten gsum la / /
dang ba'i sems kyis mchod bstod @# / /
lhur len rnams / /
tshe ring nang med bde skyid ldan pa dang / /
'gro kun sangs rgyas myur thob 'phrin las mdzod / /
badzra sa ma ya tiShTHa /
zhes pa 'di ni gcen lung mkha' spyod mkhan po bsod nams phyogs glang gis nan tan chen pos bskul ngor gshin rje'i gshed kyi rnal 'byor ba blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
! swasti /
rgyal kun ngo bo blo bzang grags pa dang / /
skyabs kyi dam pa blo bzang ye shes zhabs / /
dbyer med gsol 'debs byang chub ma thob bar / /
'bral med rdzes zungs mchog thun dngos grub stsol / /
brtan pa'i 'khor lo 'jigs mdzad gdugs dkar mo / /
las gshin 'dod khams dbang mo beg rtse can / /
dge bsnyen chen por lha btsun mi nor 'khor / /
bcol lo 'phrin las rnam bzhis skyong bar mdzod / /
ces pa 'di ni lha btsun rab 'byams pa blo bzang yar 'phel gyis 'di lta bu zhig dgos zhes bskul ba'i ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
! na mo gu ru many+dzu g+ho ShA ya /
dus gsum rgyal ba'i mkhyen brtse yon tan kun / /
gcig tu bsdus pa bka' drin gsum ldan rje / /
dur smrig gar rol mchog thun dngos grub kun / /
stsol mdzad yid bzhin nor bu'i zhabs la 'dud / /
de la 'dir bla ma'i rnal 'byor bsgom par 'dod pas dge sems khyad par can gyi ngang nas skyabs 'gro sems skyed tshad med bzhi bsgom pa sngon du btang nas 'di ltar /
rang nyid zhe sdang rdo rje yab yum du / /
gsal ba'i thugs ka'i hUM las 'od zer 'phros / /
snod bcud ma dag dri ma kun sbyangs te / /
dag ba'i zhing gyur lha dang lha mos khyab / /
lus mchog brtas byed 'dod yon lnga ldan pa'i / /
sna tshogs mchod pa'i bye brag spyan gzigs tshogs / /
lha rdzas las grub gnam sa'i khyon gang ba / /
zag med kun bzang mchod sprin rgya mtshor gyur / /
oM AHhUM /
lan gsum brjod pas byin gyis brlabs / /
de nas /
rang gi smin mtshams thad drang drang nam mkha'i ngos / /
gtsug phud lnga pas bteg pa'i 'phang mtho'i khri / /
rin chen gzar bu du mas rnam spras steng / /
'dab stong nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor rgyas pa'i dbus / /
gsum ldan bla ma rgyal kun ngo bo nyid / /
rdo rje 'chang dngos rnam pa dge slong tshul / /
sku mdog dkar dmar zhi zhing dgyes 'dzum ldan / /
zhal gcig phyag gnyis phyag g.yas chos 'chad dang / /
g.yon pa mnyam gzhag drang srong snod mchog bsnams / /
nyi gzhon 'char ka'i mdangs ldan chos gos gsum / /
legs par gsol zhing paN zhwas dbu la mdzes / /
rmad byung mtshan dang dpye byang dpal 'bar ba'i / /
'ja' 'od gur khyim 'khrigs pa'i dbus dag tu / /
zhabs gnyis rdo rje skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'i / /
phung khams rnam dag bde gshegs yab yum lnga / /
skye mched rtsa rgyus tshigs rnams byang @# / /
sems dngos / /
ba spu dgra bcom yan lag khro dbang nyid / /
mtha' skor dngos brgyud bla ma'i tshogs rnams dang / /
rgyud sde bzhi 'brel yi dam lha yi tshogs / /
sangs rgyas byang sems nyan rang dpa' bo dang / /
mkha' 'gro bstan srungs rgya mtshos bskor nas bzhugs / /
de dag gnas gsum rdo rje gsum mtshan pa'i / /
hUM yig 'od kyis chos sku'i gnas mchog nas / /
rang rang ye shes ba rnams skad cig gis / /
spyan drangs dam tshig sems dpa' so so la / /
dgye shing thims pas tshul chu bzhag bzhin / /
dbyer med gcig gyur bdag cag mos ldan 'gro'i / /
bsod nams zhing mchog nyid du brtan par bzhugs / /
de nas yan lag bdun pa 'bul ba ni /
dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i bdag po rdo rje 'chang / /
snyigs dus nyam thag mgon med 'gro ba rnams / /
sgrol phyir ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i tshul 'chang ba / /
mtshungs med rje btsun bla mar phyag 'tshal lo / /
srid zhi'i dpal 'byor las 'ongs mchod pa'i rdzas / /
rin chen maN+Dal kun bzang mchod sprin la / /
rab 'gran mchod pa'i bye brag bsam mi khyab / /
skyabs gnas kun 'dus ngo bo mnyes phyir 'bul / /
gdod nas da lta'i bar bsags mi dge'i las / /
gnong zhing 'gyod pas bla ma lha tshogs drung / /
mi 'chab bsam pa thag pas bshags bgyid cing / /
slan chad mi dge'i las rnams yang dag sdom / /
chos kun rang bzhin gyis grub bden bral yang / /
sgyu ma smig rgyu chu zla ji bzhin du / /
skye 'phags kun gyis bsags pa'i rnam dkar dger / /
bdag ni bsam pa thag pas rjes yi rang / /
rang rang gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa bzhin / /
phan dang bde ba ma lus 'byung ba'i gnas / /
zab dang rgya che'i chos 'khor bla med pa / /
rtag par rgyun chad med par bskor bar bskul / /
chos skur 'gyur med skye 'chi dang bral yang / /
tha mal tshul bzung ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i sku / /
mar gyur smin grol lam la 'god slad du / /
'khor ba ma stongs par du rtag bzhugs gsol / /
'dis mtshon bdag dang gzhan gyis dus gsum du / /
bsags pa'i phul byung bsod nams ci mchis pa / /
'gro kun byang chub mchog la dgod bya'i phyir / /
zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang chen thob phyir bsngo /
zhes yan lag bdun pa phul nas skyabs gnas bslu ba med pa'i bdag nyid du mos te ra sa gzhan na med pa'i blo ltos bcas la kha tsam tshig tsam ma yin par gdung shugs drag po'i sgo nas rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma gang yin gyi gsol 'debs gang lcogs byas pa'i mthar /
yon tan kun 'byung tshul khrims zhing sa la / /
rnam dag bslab gsum ljon pa'i lo 'dab rgyas / /
nges 'byung byang chub sems kyi 'bras bus brjid / /

rgyal kun mkhyen brtse'i zlos gar las 'ongs pa'i / /
@# / /
gang sku bde gshegs rigs lnga byang sems sogs / /

bde ldan zhing sogs phyogs bcu'i zhing khams nas / /

'khor bcas thogs pa med par gshegs su gsol / /

! na mo gu gu many+dzu g+ho ShU ya /
rje rgyal ba kun gyi ye shes nyid / /
pha mtshungs med drin can bla ma'i zhabs / /
sprang bdag snying padmo'i dbus bzhugs la /
blo chos la phyogs par byin gyis rlobs / /
rten dal brgyad 'byor bcu tshang ba'i lus / /
'di thob dka' jig sla'i tshul mthong na / /
da don med bya bas mi 'da' bar / /
don snying po len par mi rigs sam / /
dkor nor rdzas sbrang ma'i sbrang rtsi dang / /

srog brtan med nam mkha'i glog dang mtshungs / /
da 'khor ba'i gnas la chags pa 'khrul / /

lar skad cig nyid la 'jig 'gyur zhing / /
kun mi 'dod 'chi bdag khar chud na / /

lus longs spyod gnyen 'khor dbus gnas kyang / /
skyabs re sa bral ba'i bar do'i 'phrad / /
yid 'phyo zhing gcig pur 'gro ba'i che / /
skyabs dam chos min pa cang 'dug gam / /
sngon thog med dus nas da lta'i bar / /

blo gzu bor gnas pas legs brtags nas / /
da sdig spong dge ba'i las rnams la / /

mar @# / /
gyur pa'i sems can mtha' yas par / /
byams snying rje byang chub sems bskyed cing / /
rje rgyal ba'i thugs kyi zab don dang / /
rgya che ba'i chos la 'bad rtsol dgos / /
dus rtag tu bsten na srid zhi yi / /
dpal 'dod dgu'i 'byor pa mchog ster ba'i / /
nor 'phags nor bdun gyi mdzod bzang po / /
da lus grib bzhin du bsten ra ran / /
drin che ba'i sems can pha ma la / /
byams snying rje ldan pa'i sems bskyed nas /

yid gus pas bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / /

don med pa'i bya bas 'da' gyur na / /

da yengs med bag dang ldan par byos / /
rje rgyal ba gong ma'i rnam thar bzhin / /

ma 'gro kun byang chen rgyu ru bsngo /

bskal bzang rnam 'dren bzhi pa thub dbang gi /
ngo mtshar brgya phrag zlos gar 'khrungs rabs kyi / /

rnam 'dren thugs rje'i spyi gzugs tsong kha pa / /
bslab gsum rgyan mdzes blo bzang ye shes zhabs / /
pad dkar 'dzin pa skal bzang rgya mtsho'i sde / /

'gro rnams byams pas skyong la gsol ba 'debs / /

skye rabs du mar chu yi gzegs ma ltar / /
nyer bsags tshogs gnyis rgya mtsho las thon zhing / /
phun tshogs yon tan ldan pa'i 'od dkar can / /
gdul bya'i ku mud bzhad la gsol ba 'debs /
dag la dbang bsgyur blo gros gzhal med khang / /
byams dang snying rje lhag bsam nor gyis bltams / /
'gro la chos sbyin rgya cher spel mdzad pa'i / /

zung 'jug go 'phang myur du thob par shog /
