mgon khyod gang du bzhugs kyang mi ngal zhing / /
mtha' klas 'gro ba'i don las ma mchis kyang / /
bdag sogs mos blo'i kun+da'i tshal 'byed phyir / /
yang srid mchog sprul zla ba myur ston gsol / /
mchog gsum ngo bo 'jam mgon cing kha pa'i / /
byin rlabs dam can rgya mtsho'i mthu stobs kyis / /
snying nas gsol btab ji ltar smon pa'i don / /
gegs med myur du 'grub pa nyid gyur cig /
ces tsha khang no min khang ngag dbang blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i sprul sku myur phebs kyi gsol 'debs shig dgos zhes er te ne sde ba dang / /
sde pa u'i ja'i sang /
rab 'byams pa bcas slob 'khor tshang mas bskul ba'i ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
! swa sti /
mkhyen brtse gting dpag dka' ba'i chu gter che / /
rnam dag bslab gsum rim gnyis nor gyis gang / /
gzhan phan 'phrin las rlabs 'phreng cher g.yo ba'i / /
mtshungs med rje btsun bla mar gsol ba 'debs / /
rmad byung thugs bskyed bzang po'i lha lam las / /
byams dang snying rje'i char rgyun legs phab ste / /
'gro ba'i dug gsum tsha gdung bcil mkhas pa'i / /
gtan gyi skyabs gnas khyod la gsol pa 'debs / /
de ltar gsol btab mthu las bla ma yis / /
bstan 'dzin chos dkar skye srid thams cad du / /
rjes bzungs ngal brgyad 'byor bcu'i rten thub nas / /
zung 'jug bde chen go 'phang myur thob shog /
ces pa 'di ni zhus dag pa dka' chen mkhas btsun gyi ma'i 'dod smon du btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / /
! swa sti /
phul byung blo gros yangs pa'i mkha' dbyings su / /
'phrin las bzang po'i dkyil 'khor rab rgyas shing / /
ye shes snang bas phyogs kun khyab mdzad pa / /
skal bzang 'dab brgya'i gnyen mchog zhabs brtan shog / /
blo gter dur smrig gar rol ring lugs gzhir / /
bslab gsum ljon pa bzang po'i rtsa ba brtan / /
ye shes yal 'dab 'bras bu g.yur za ba'i / /
rje btsun dpag bsam dbang po zhabs brtan shog /
rmad byung bde legs 'byung gnas gsang ri las / /
rgya chen 'phrin las 'chad med dal 'gro'i rgyun / /
nyer phab 'gro blo'i rgya mtsho yongs 'gangs shing / /
phan bde'i rlabs 'phreng g.yo la gsol ba 'debs / /
mchog gsum byin rlabs drang srong bden pa'i tshig /
grub pa'i smon pa bstan srungs mthu rtsal dang / /
dad ldan gdul byas gsol btab rten 'brel mthus / /
bstan pa'i nyer 'tshor rtag bzhugs gsol ba 'debs / /
thub bstan spyi dang 'jam mgon tsong kha pa'i / /
ring lugs mthar khyab bla nas blar 'phel zhing / /
@# / /
ljongs 'dir nad mtshon nyer 'tshe rab zhi nas / /
bde skyid legs tshogs 'phel pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di ni pa'i si pho lha nas kyis rgyun par kha ton dang gzhan la spel chog pa zhig dgos zhes nan gyis bskul ba ltar shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
! swa sti /
tshogs gnyis yongs rdzogs mtshan dpe'i gzi 'bar ba'i / /
rgyal dang de'i gsung de sgrub dge 'dun bcas / /
skye rgu yongs kyi bsod nams zhing mchog la / /
lus ngag yid gsum dang bas phyag bgyid do / /
thub dbang gnas brtan bcu drug bde gshegs brgyad / /
sher phyin zab don 'chad mkhas rab 'byor che'i / /
'khrungs rabs snang brnyan gzi byin rab 'bar dang / /
grub pa'i dbang phyug rgyal ba dben sa pa / /
yab sras gsung zab gces mjod pu sta ka /
sdom btson bsod nams lhun grub lhag bsam gyis / /
bskrun pa 'dis mtshon bdag gzhan thams cad kyi / /
dus gsum rnam dkar dge tshogs gcig bsdus mthus / /
rje b+tshun blo zang ye shes dpal bzang po / /
mi gzhig rdo rje ltar brtan khri 'phang rtser / /
bskal brgyar mi g.yo mtha' klas yid can 'gro'i / /
bsam pa dang mthun chos 'khor bskor bar shog /
gzhan yang dge 'dis mkhas mang 'du ba'i gnas / /
mda' pa bkra shis lhun po'i dge 'dun tshogs / /
thugs mthun khrims gtsang nor bdun gyis phyug cing / /
'khor lo gsum gyis nyin mtshan 'da' bar shog /
mchog gsum bla mar ba gyid mdzad chos kyi rgyal / /
blo bzang padma sku tshe rab brtan cing / /
rigs brgyud mda' thad legs 'phel srid brtan sogs / /
thugs bzhed ma lus lhun gyis grub gyur cig /
bdag sogs deng nas tshe rabs thams cad du / /
rje btsun bla mas 'bral med rjes ba zungs nas / /
ma 'ongs drag po 'khor lo can gyur tshe / /
'khor gyi dang por skye ba'i bkra shis shog /
ces mda' pa bkra shis lhun po'i bla ma rab 'byams smra ba bsod nams lhun grub kyis sku rten dang /
gsung rten 'ga' zhig bzhengs pa'i 'dod smon tshogs 'don du btsugs cho ga pa zhig dgos zhes nan gyis bskul ba la brten nas chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
! oM swa sti /
kye| rdo rje 'chang s+chen rtsa brgyud bla ma yi / /
bka' sdod rgyal po chen po mthu stobs can / /
'phrin las bsgrub phyir gnas mchog dam pa 'dir / /
spyan 'dren 'khor bcas ma yengs gshegs su gsol / /
sku mdog shel ltar rab 'tsher srog gi bdag /
zhal gcig phyag gnyi dang mdur ral gri bsnams / /
bse khrab gsol zhing ye shes spyan gcig pa / /
rdzu 'phrul gdong lda'i steng du brtan par bzhugs / /
dngos bshams yid sprul phyi nang mchod pa'i sprin / /
dam rdzas sha khrag gser skyems gtor tshogs dang / /
spyan gzigs @# / /
'dod dgu'i 'byor ba bsam mi khyab / /
sbyangs rtogs sbar byas 'khor bcas khyed la 'bul / /
dung ltar dkar ba'i pho brang dam pa nas / /
gang 'tsham thabs kyi sprul pa sna tshogs pas / /
bstan dgra dam nyams ma lus brlag mdzad pa'i / /
bka' yi rgyal chen 'khor dang bcas la bstod / /
snyigs dus 'jam mgon bstan dang bstan 'dzin la / /
log lta'i dgra bgegs nyer 'cho kun choms la / /
rnal 'byor bdag cag mi nor 'khor dang bcas / /
'phrin las rnam bzhis bu bzhin skyong bar mdzod /
ces pa 'di ni dga' ldan rab rgyas bla ma bka' chen don grub rgya mtshos chos bdag rgyal po chen po la 'phrin 'cho la zhig dgos zhes bskul ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / /
! 'dul ba lung la /
na maHshAkya mu na ye /
don kun grub pa'i thugs kyi bcud phyung ba / /
bstan pa'i snying po 'dul ba lung sde bzhi / /
kun+da ltar dkar shog bu'i ngos yangs su / /
mgon po bkra shis stobs rgyas lhag bsam gyis / /
gzugs su bgyis pa'i dge tshogs rlabs chen mthus / /
rgyu sbyor nye 'brel 'khor dang bcas pa rnams / /
tshe ring nad med dpal 'byor legs 'phel zhing / /
rtag tu ngal 'byor tshang ba'i rten thob shog /
gdod nas nyer bsags bsod nams sa bon bzang / /
dal 'byor tshul khrims ldan pa'i gzhir skyes ljon / /
nges legs 'bras bu'i khur gyis rab dud par / /
mar gyur 'gro kun ci dgar spyod gyur cig /
! sher phyogs la /
chos kun rang bzhin gyis stong mtha' bral don / /
legs par ston pa thub pa'i gsung zab mo / /
dus gsum rgyal kun bskyed yum pha rol phyin / /
ri mor bgyis la mthun sbyor grogs byed rnams / /
sgrib byang rgyal ba'i dgongs don legs rtogs nas / /
gzung 'dzin 'khrul pa'i tshang tshing stug po'i tshogs / /
bdag med shes rab me chen gyis bsregs te / /
bde chen ye shes snang ba rab rgyas shog /
! phal po che la /
thub gsung phal chen bla mar bgyis pa'i mthus / /
stobs bcu mnga' kun mtshan brjod phan yon sogs / /
bdag sogs skye rgu kun gyi yid dbang du / /
nyer sim phan bde'i dpal la spyod par shog /
gzhan yang dge 'dis yon bdag rigs rgyud bcas / /
nyer 'tshe kun bral rigs 'byor 'bru 'phel zhing / /
dal brgyad 'byor bcu'i rten bzang legs brgyud nas / /
thams cad gzigs pa'i go 'phang myur thob shog /
! dkon brtsegs la /
srid zhi'i bde la chags pa rab spangs nas / /
mkha' mnyam 'gro ba srid pa'i rgya mtsho las / /
stobs bcu mnga' ba'i sa ru 'khrid pa'i khur / /
lci ba mi 'dor khyer ba'i byang sems las / /
brtsams te gsungs pa dkon brtsegs pusta ka /
yid can bsod nams gsog pa'i rten mchog tu / /
bgyis pa 'dis mtshon dge tshogs ci mchis pa / /
@# / /
'gro kun don du byang chub chen por bsngo / /
! /
mdo mang la /
mi mjed zhing gtso zas gtsang sras po yis / /
chos 'khor rim pa gsum du bskor ba las / /
de gsum ci rigs gtogs pa'i chos dkon mchog /
glegs bur bgyis pa 'dis mtshon bdag dang gzhan / /
skye 'phags kun gyis dus gsum du bsags ba'i / /
kun+da dung ltar rab dkar dge tshogs mthus / /
ljongs 'dir nad mtshon mu ge mi mthun phyogs / /
nyer zhi rdzogs ldan dpal la longs spyod shog /
! myang 'das la /
rtag 'dzin can rnams gdul phyir mya ngan las / /
'da' tshul bstan tshe gsungs pa myang 'das tshe / /
bla mar bgyis pa'i bsod nams phung po gang / /
'gro kun myang 'das thob pa'i rgyu ru bsngo / /
! rgyud 'bum pa /
gdul bya rigs bzhi'i bsam pa dang mthun par / /
rgyal bas rgyud sde rnam pa bzhir gsungs pa / /
bzhengs pa'i dge bas bdag dang ma rgan 'gro /
ring min rdo rje 'chang chen thob phyir bsngo / /
gangs can ljongs 'dir thub gsung 'gyur ro 'tshal / /
glegs bam bcu phrag bcu dang brgyad lhag pa / /
gzugs su bgyis la mthun sbyar bgyid sogs 'gro /
sdig ltung kun byang gnas skabs bde ldan zhing / /
mthar thug kun mkhyen go 'phang thob pa dang / /
rgyu sbyor 'khor bcas tshe ring nad med cing / /
rigs rgyud mnga' thang bla nas blar 'phel te / /
dal 'byor rten brgyud sangs rgyas myur thob shog /
ces pa rnam pad tshal nas mgon po bkra shis stobs rgyas kyis rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro 'tshal bzhengs skabs 'dod smon tshigs su bcad pa zhig dgos zhes bskul ba ltar shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
sarba dza ga tam / /
! swasti /
bcos bu'i dz+hai k+ShiM las bsgrubs ngo mtshar rmad byung snang mtha'i sku mchog 'dir / /
nang gzhug ring bsrel rnam gsum rten mang dang bcas blo bzang ye shes kyis / /
legs bskrun ye shes pa bstim bsod nams zhing mchog bsgrubs pa 'dis mtshon dges / /
rgyu sbyor ye shes bstan 'dzin bde ldan zhing der thogs med rab bgrong shog /
ces pa 'di ni sa khud pa ye shes bstan 'dzin gyis rgyal ba 'od dpag med kyi snang brnyan bcos ma'i j+ho k+ShiM las bzhengs pa'i rgyab yig tu bgyis pa'o / /
sarba mang+ga laM / /
! swasti /
blo bzang rgyal ba'i ring lugs kha ba'i spor / /
mi 'jigs dbang bsgyur dpal ldan gdong lnga pa / /
lung rigs chos phung snyan grags cher sgrogs pa'i / /

thos bsam sgom pa'i rlung shugs ches drag pas / /

@# / /

rnam 'dren kun dngos blo bzang grags pa yi / /

khal kha /
khod bcas ser skya thun mong nas bskul ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / /
! na mo gu ru bud+d+ha po d+hi satwA ya /
mi mjed zhing gi ston bzas gtsang sras / /
gang gi lung rtogs bstan pa nyin mo lar / /
gsal mdzad 'jam mgon bla ma tsong kha pa / /
yab sras brgyud par bcas la gus phyag 'tshal / /

stobs kyis / /
'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa'i / /
lung rtogs bstan pa phyogs bcur rgyas pa dang / /
de nyid 'dzin cing spel la mi zhum pa'i / /
rlabs chen thugs 'char skyes bu ma lus pa'i / /

'dzin ma'i khyon kun yongs su khyab gyur cig /
pha mar gyur pa'i 'gro ba ma lus kyang / /

rdzogs byang myur du thob pa nyid gyur cig /

med shog /

bshad sgrub rnam par dkar ba'i 'phrin las kyis / /
skal bzang gdul bya thar lam bkri mkhas pa'i / /
mkhyen rab dbang phyug zhabs la gsol ba 'debs / /
dri med bslab gsum sdom pas rgyud gtams shing / /
sgo gsum dge la 'dun pa'i rnam dpyod dang / /
bag yod nges 'byung byang sems kyis phyug pa'i / /

'gro mgon zhabs zung bskal brgyar g.yo med cing / /
zab rgyas chos 'khor rgyun chad med skor shog /

! oM swasti /
rnam dpyod yon tan kun 'byung blo mchog rgyas / /
skal bzang gdul bya'i 'dren pa bla na med / /

bzhin chad med rgyun skyong ba / /
yang dag bsgom la brtson par byin x / /

sdig spong dge ba'i las kun mtha' dag la / /
'jug pa dam pa'i spyod pa skyong bar shog /
rnam dag dbang bzhi gang+gA'i chu rgyun gyis / /

'jam dpal snying pos bdag nyid tshe rabs kun / /

! swasti /
thub bstan dri med gsal mdzad 'jam mgon rje / /

! oM swasti /
rig grol gnyis ldan dge bcur spyod pa'i gnas / /
dga' ldan rab rgyas 'dus tshogs dgyes bskyed rten / /
btung ba'i snod mchog rin chen las bskrun dges / /
thugs mthun khrims gtsang dge bcur rtag rol shog /
ces pa 'di yang dga' ldan rab rgyas su tshogs khro gsar du bskrun pa'i zhal yig tu btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis bgyis pa'o / /
! oM bde legs su gyur cig /
chos 'khor bde chen khrims ldan 'dus pa'i tshogs / /
mnyes byed btung ba'i yol go yid 'ong ba / /
legs bsgrubs 'dis mtshon dus gsum dge ba'i mthus /
nyin mtshan 'khor lo gsum gyis 'da' bar shog /
ces pa 'di yang rgyal chen rtse chos 'khor sde chen du tshogs khro gsar bskrun bgyis pa'i zhal byang du dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
! 'dul lung rnams la /

! 'bum rnams la /

gzung 'dzin rnam rtog dbyings las grol bar shog /
! nyi khri rnams la /
zab mo'i don ston nyi khri lnga stong rnams / /

! khri brgyad stong pa rnams la /

sher phyin 'bring po'i pusta ka bzhengs par / /
sgo gsum mthun rkyen bsgrub pa'i lus can dang / /
yon bdag sdig sgrib nyes ltung kun byang shog /
! shes rab khri par /
thabs mkhas thub pa'i dbang po'i dgongs zab mchog /

bzhengs pa'i rnam dkar dge bas bdag gzhan kun / /
bden 'dzin 'khor ba'i gnas las grol bar shog /
! brgyad stong pa la /

le'u so gnyis glegs bur rab bskrun pas / /
bdag sogs pha mar gyur pa'i 'gro ba kun / /
sgrib byang yum chen go 'phang myur thob shog /
! sna tshogs khri par /

! phal chen rnams la /
tha ma chos 'khor bskor ba las byung ba'i / /

bzhengs pa'i dge ba pad rtsa ltar dkar bas / /
lus can 'khor ba'i mtsho las sgrol bar shog /
! dkon brtsegs rnams la /

! mdo mang rnams la /

! myang 'das la /

! rgyud 'bum rnams la /
u duM wA ra'i me tog las dkon pa'i / /

skal bzang gdul byar stsol ba'i bu sta ka /

kun la ma 'dris mdza' bshes stobs bcu pas / /
'gro la brtser dgongs rgyu 'bras theg pa'i bka' / /
mtshungs med lo paN rnams kyi bka' drin las / /

! oM swasti /
bgrang yas bskal par rlabs chen spyod pa yis / /

'dren mchog shAkya'i tog der mgos phyag 'tshal / /

'khor los bsgyur @# / /
rgyal 'jam dbyangs gong ma'i bkas / /
mtho ron pad li'i mtshan bcas bod 'bangs spyi'i / /
mi rjer dbang bskur gang gis ljon shing logs / /
par brko'i thugs bskyed yongs grub rnam dkar mthus / /
sku tshe chab srid mnga' thang rgyas gyur cig /

! na mo gu ru shAkya mu na ye /
mkha' mnyam 'gro ba'i phan bde 'byung ba'i gnas / /

gdon bgegs dpung 'joms khro rgyal dpal rta mgrin / /
tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor los rig 'dzin stsol / /
rmugs 'dzin nor 'chang beg tse dgra bgegs sgrol / /
gnas 'di bsrung skyob dar rgyas dge bsnyen che / /
rgyal ba rgya mtsho nyan thos bsrung tshogs sogs / /
ngo mtshar snang brnyan mig gi bdud rtsi'i dpyid / /
dbu mdzad dar rgyas rgyal mtshan grogs bcas kyis / /
yid gzhungs sor mo'i zlos gar ngag gis bskrun / /
skye 'phags khrims ldan dge 'dun 'dus tshogs kyi / /
thugs dam zab mo'i spyan rten yid 'ong ba / /
sna tshogs gos bzang mang pos rab spras shing / /
legs byas zhing gi mchog tu rab tu bsngags / /
dge mtshan rnam par bkra bas phyogs kun shis / /
lhun po bzhin du mi g.yo 'dus gling gi /
kun dga' ra ba'i mthongs skor khor mo yug /
bsam pas kun nas rab tu mdzes par byas / /
bskal bzang bzhi pa'i ring lugs 'dab brgya'i tshal / /
'byed la blo gros 'od stong 'dus pa'i sde / /
ma pham 'byon min ri dbang ltar brtan cing / /
zhwa ser bstan pa bla nas blar 'phel shog /
'dis mtshon bdag gzhan dge ba bad rtsa ltar / /
dkar bas sa gsum gtogs so cog gi 'gro /
dal 'byor rten thob ring min thar pa'i lam / /
brgyud nas sku gsum gzhal med khang 'jug shog /
skye dgu'i ma 'dris mdza' bshes rdzogs sangs rgyas / /
thog mtha' bar gsum dge ba dam pa'i chos / /
tshul bzhin bsgrub mdzad tshangs spyod dge 'dun gyis / /
srid zhi ma lus khyab pa'i bkra shis shog / / /

swasti /
rab 'byams zhing gi sangs rgyas sras slob bcas / /
bkra shis lhun po'i byang chub snying po'i gnas / /
ye shes sems dpa' dngos byon gzugs sku dang / /
dbyer med skyabs gsum 'dus pa'i spyan snga ru / /
bdag nyid ring mo nyid nas khyu mchog gi /
bya ba cung zad bsags pa'i rnam smin gyi / /
'bras bu dkar por 'dzag pa da lta'i skabs / /
phyogs kun nas 'dus mos pa sna tshogs kyis / /
bstabs pa'i rin chen du ma las byung ba'i / /
dra pa dra phyed rab 'phyang rgyan 'phreng dang / /
'phan gzugs ngos la mchod pa'i bye brag sogs / /
mu tig rin chen dag gis legs par bsgrubs / /
stong 'khun gan mdzod la sogs yul gru nas / /

grangs med rgyal bas 'gro la thugs rjes gzigs / /
rang lus grangs med rdul dang mnyam sbrul nas / /
slu med skyabs yul tshogs la phyag 'tshal zhing / /
kun bzang mchod sprin sa dang bar snang bkang / /
dgyes ba bskyed phyir dang bas dbul bar bgyi / /
thog med dus nas nyon mongs sdig ltung kun / /
gnyen po stobs bzhi'i sgo nas bshags shing sdom / /
bdag gzhan dge ba byas dang byed bzhin pa / /

dus gsum rnam 'dren slob mar bcas pa'i tshogs / /

skye dgu kun la snyoms pa mchog gsum gyi / /

'jig rten spyi dang kha bas yongs bskor ljongs / /
'gro ba'i bsod nams kun gsal la 'char shog /
tshangs spyod bslab gsum ldan pa 'dus ba'i sdes / /

bshad sgrub rnam par dkar ba'i bya ba la / /
skad cig tsam yang brtson pa mi dman shog rgyal ba gnyis pa 'jam dpal snying po yi / /

gyen du 'degs mdzad khrims ldan dge 'dun tshogs / /
'chad rtsod rtsom la rtag tu gzhol bar shog /
skyabs @# / /
yul kun gyi mkhyen brtse'i mthu dpung gis / /

rdzogs ldan dpal la spyod pa'i bkra shis shog /

spungs / /

de yang /

ma bsgoms gyur kyang ltud med na / /

tshogs la brgya phyag /

mtshams pa @# / /

shug las /

dge 'dun rnams nas kyang spyod lam thams cad du dran dang shes bzhin bag dang ldan par mdzad cing /

sgom sgrub kyi myong ba thon pa /
gzhan phan 'phrin las la brtson pa lhur bzhes kyis rang gzhan ris med mtha' dag gi rgyud la lung rtogs kyi bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas pa dang /
srid zhi'i legs tshogs ma lus pa 'phel ba'i thabs la thugs bsam rnam par dag pa'i khur bzhes 'tshal /
de ltar blang dor tshul bzhin bsgrub pa rnams @# / /
la /
bstan srungs ngam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyis 'phrin las rnam bzhis g.yel med skyong ba dang /
bsam spyor ngan pa'i sgo nas lta ngan log sgrub byed pa rnams la tshar gcod rjes 'dzin mdzod cig /
gtsug lag khang rnams klog pa dang / /
kha ton gyis rgyas legs gnas shog /
rtag tu dge 'dun mthun pa dang / /
dge 'dun don yang 'grub par shog /
sarba mang+galaM / / /
!swasti /
rnam 'dren kun gyi yab gyur gzhon nu'i tshul / /
byams dang snying rje'i 'od kyis chab 'bangs kyi / /
tsha gdung kun sel dge legs kun+da'i tshal / /
rgyas mdzad kun phan chos rgyal rtag brtan shog /
rgyal pa stong gi mchog gyur shAkya'i tog /
bstan pa rin chen dbyar mtsho ltar spel zhing / /
'dzam gling bde legs chen pos khyab mdzad pa'i / /
mi bdag sku che g.yung drung lta bur shog /
'jam dpal snying po'i bstan pa phan bde'i gzhi / /
sri zhur brtson mdzad gnam bskos bdag po yi / /
mnga' thang chab srid dpal 'byor legs tshogs rnams / /
yar ngo'i zla bzhin gong nas gong 'phel shog /
khyu mchog rlabs chen las 'ongs stobs 'khor bsgyur / /
mang bkur khri la lugs brgya'i sgo 'phar phye / /
chab 'bangs khrims kyis bde bar rab bskyangs nas / /
rdzogs ldan dpal gyi dus ltar spyod gyur cig /
dkon mchog thugs rje bstan srungs mthu rtsal dang / /
drang srong bden mthus rgya hor bod yul kun / /
nad mug 'khrug rtsod mi 'dod kun zhi zhing / /
sring zhi'i dge mtshan stsol pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces ba 'di ni gong ma bdag po chan po'i zham ring ba me ren cang gi dge 'dun chos 'phel gyis lha mi'i gtsug rgyan 'jam dbyangs gong ma rgyal po'i brtan bzhugs 'dod gsol chigs bcad cig dgos zhes bskul ba ltar shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis bka' gdams pho brang du smras pa'o / /
mang+galaM / /
! swasti /
rgyal ba kun las cher bsngags pad dkar bzhin / /
bu ram shing pa'i chos tshul bla na med / /
tshul bzhin nyams su len la zla bral ba / /
phan bda'i lam ston bka' gdams shing rta'i srol / /
ji bzhin 'byed mdzad legs pa'i shes rab dang / /
blo ldan shes rab mkhas grub rim byon gyis / /
bshad sgrub bya bas thub bstan gsal ba'i gnas / /
dpal gsang ne'u thog gi dgon gnas kyi / /
bsti gnas gan+d+ho la der byi dor dang / /
gser gyi lhun po la 'gran gser zangs las / /
grub pa'i rgya phigs ngo mtshar gzi byin 'bar / /
blta bas mi bzongs sa phyogs 'od kyis 'gengs / /
sprul sku blo bzang bstan pas phu dung kyis / /
bdog pa'i dngos 'byor spungs pa'i rgyu sbyar zhing / /
mthun @# / /
sbyor mi dbang bsod nams stobs rgyas kyis / /
mngon par ldang pa'i sgo nas legs bar bsgrubs / /
'dis mchon dge tshogs ston ka'i 'od dkar bzhin / /
dkar ba gang des rdog lo khu dpon dang / /
bdag nyid chen po'i bstan dang nge 'dzin rnams / /
ma pham 'byon min bar du g.yo med shog /
bsil ljongs zhwa ser lags gnyis bstan pa'i gdugs / /
gyen du legs 'degs mi dbang chos rgyal gyi / /
sku tshe mnga' thang chab sring rtag brtan cing / /
'chi med dbang po'i dpal la 'gran gyur cig /
'di'i ched sgo gsum 'bad par gtogs so cog /
byang chub bar du legs tshogs kun grub pa / /
gtan mdun thar pa'i khang bzang ram pa der / /
myur 'jug skal ba bzang por 'gyur bar shog /
mdo khams bkra shis chos rdzong ma lag dgon / /
bla slob bslab gsum ldan pa'i 'dus pa'i tshogs / /
'jam mgon bla ma'i gzhung lugs spel ba la / /

dgon gnas dge 'dun 'khor dang longs sbyod rnams / /
'phrin las rnam bzhis g.yel med skyong bar mdzod / /

bkra shis rgya mtshos phyogs kun khyab bar shog /

! swasti /
bla ma yi dam mthu ldan chos srungs dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs rnams la / /

! swasti /
blo mchog thub pa'i mdo rgyud gang+ga'i yab / /

@# / /
'gyur med tshe mtha' yas pa'i ngo bo bzhin / /

'og min zhing gtso'i mgon po ltar brtan shog /

zla med rje btsun bla mar gsol ba 'debs / /

byung ba'i 'phrin las bzang po'i dpal mnga' ba / /

bshes gnyen bzang bo'i zhabs la /

lung rigs chos kyi rgyal mtshan cher bsgreng ba'i / /
lhag bsam bsam 'phel nor bu'i tog gis mdzes / /
bstan pa rgyas bar mdzad la X blo gsal skal bzang 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams la / /
zab don gsal par ston la rab mkhas pa / /
lung rtogs dar zhing rgyas pa'i rnam dpyod can / /
zla med dpal ldan bla mar X byams dang snying rje kun bzod ma yi gzhir / /
lhag bsam byang sems ljon pa'i me tog mdzes / /
don gnyis rnam bar rgyal ba'i 'bras bus brjid / /
gdul bya'i re ba skong la X dpal ldan mi mjed snying bo'i bstan pa la / /
rnam dag tshangs spyod ngur smig gos kyis klubs / /
rtag par chos 'khor bskor ba'i grags pa can / /
yongs 'dzin dam pa'i zhabs la X rgyud snge'i gzhung lugs rin chen 'byung gnas las / /
zab lam rim gnyis yid bzhin dbang gi rgyal / /
phun sum tshogs pa'i dgos 'dod ma lus pa / /
stsol mdzad dpal ldan bla mar X rgyal ba gnyis pa'i lugs bzang gangs ri'i spor / /
'chad rtsod ral pas mtshan pa'i mche snger bgrad / /
lung rigs lus stobs rgyas pa'i seng ge'i rtsal / /
'jigs bral dge ba'i bshes la X shes bya kun la nam mkha' ltar yangs pa / /
mkhyen brtse'i rlung gis shing rta lang long g.yo / /
phan bde'i gru char bzang po gdul bya la / /
'bebs mdzad bshes gnyen dam par X rgyal dang rgyal ba gnyis pa'i thugs kyi bcud / /
nyi zla ltar grags gsang sngags rdo rje theg /
zab dang rgya che'i snang byed 'od po che / /
skal bzang padmo'i tshal rab rgyas byed pa / /
rig grol yon tan ldan pa 'dus pa'i tshogs / /
bka' dang dgongs 'grel gdams pa zab mo'i don / /
'chad dang thos bsam sgom pa ngal 'gro'i rgyun / /
byams bstan bar du chad med rab 'phel bar / /
mahA kA la chos kyi rgyal po la / /
bcol lo gtad do rnam kun dang rgyas dang / /
'phrin las rnam bzhis byang chub ma thob bar / /
rtag tu g.yel ba med pa'i grogs mdzod cig /
sngom brtson rnam dag dur smrig gos kyis brgyan / /
nges 'byung byang chub sems kyis rgyud phyug cing / /
nyin mtshan 'khor lo gsum gyis dus 'da' bar / /
shAkya'i rgyal po'i lugs bzang 'dzin par shog /
rgyal ba gnyis pa 'jam dpal snying po yi / /
dri med mdo sngags gzhung gis khams gsum khyab / /
'gro la phan bde 'byung ba'i sgo gcig pu / /
yar ngo'i zla bzhin bla nas bla 'phel shog /
'jig rten khams su mi 'dod rgud pa kun / /
zhi zhing rdzogs ldan dpal la spyod pa dang / /
skye rgu phan tshun byams pa'i sems ldan zhing / /
bla med byang chen thob pa'i @# / /
bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di ni rgyud stong grwa tshang gi bla ma 'ga' zhig gi brgyud 'debs dang /
'dod tshig smon lam bcas 'di lta bu zhig dgos zhes bla spyis bskul ba'i ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa dge legs 'phel / /
! swasti /
rgyal ba de gsung dge 'dun thugs rje'i bcud / /
rmad byung blo gros bum bzang las phyur ba'i / /
'gro ba'i sdig ltung dri ma 'khrud mdzad cing / /
brtse chen ye shes 'od 'bar zhabs brtan shog /
nyes bral bslab pa gsum gyis rgyud phyug cing / /
rnam dpyod dur smrig rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i mchog /
rgyal ba'i ring lugs phyogs brgyar spel mdzad che / /
bdag sogs bde chen 'khor lor rtag bzhugs gsol / /
thub pa'i dgongs don mthar thug rgyud gzhung la / /
legs par spyad pas zab lam rim gnyis kyi / /
rnal 'byor mthar phyin dbang phyug brgyad ldan la / /
rtse gcig gus pa'i yid kyis gsol ba 'debs / /
bcos min gdung shugs drag pos gsol btab mthus / /
rjes bzung dal 'byor rten brgyud bla med lam / /
brten nas dam sngom mig 'bras ltar bsrungs nas / /
zung 'jug go 'phang dam pa myur thob shog /
rgyal dang rgyal ba gnyis pa'i lung rtogs kyi / /
bstan pa yar do'i zla ltar rab 'phel zhing / /
skye dgu phan tshun byams pa'i sems ldan pas / /
srid gsum bde legs chen pos khyab par shog /
ces pa 'di ni 'jam dbyangs gong ma rgyal po chen po'i gser yig pa tA bla ma chos 'phel dar rgyas dang /
tA bla ma rab 'byams ba blo bzang dpal 'byor gyis rgyun gyi kha 'don zhig dgos zhes bskul ngor shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / /
! swasti /
sngon goms khyu mchog rlabs chen bzang po'i mthus / /
gnam skos 'jam dbyangs gong ma chos kyi rgyal / /
chab 'bangs rdzogs ldan gsar pa'i dga' ston la / /
sbyor mdzad rdo rje'i khril g.yo med shog /
blo chen rgyal ba gnyis btsong kha ba'i / /
bstan pa'i lam bzang ston la zla bral ba / /
ye shes 'od kyis blang dor rab gsal ba / /
'dren mchog bla ma sring mthar rtag bzhugs gsol / /
mchog gsum byin rlabs drang srong bden pa'i tshig /
dam can mthu stobs gus ldan gsol btab pa'i / /
rten 'brel phun tshogs re ba lhun grub nas / /
'gro kun bde skyid ldan pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di ni 'jam dbyangs gong ma chen po'i zham ring pa mE rin rdzang gi dge 'dun chos 'phel gyis 'di lta bu zhig dgos zhes nan gyis bskul ba ltar shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang por shes kyis sbyar ba sarba mang+ga laM / /
! thub pa'i dgongs don zab dang rgya che'i gzhung / /
blo gsal skal bzang gdul byar rnam kun tu / /
spel mdzad rgyal ba dgyes pa'i lam bzang la / /
'gong mkhas bshes gnyen bzang por gsol ba 'debs /
zhes spong ba pa dka' chen blo bzang rnam rgyal gyi gsol 'debs 'di ni /
lam rim brgyud 'debs gras su bcug chog pa zhig dgos zhes slob tshogs rnams kyis bskul ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis @# / /
smras so / /
! swasti /
bla ma rgyal ba zhi khro'i snang brnyan ras mchog kun gsal la / /
dbang gzhu ltar bkra'i ye shes mngon sum bzhugs 'dra'i bsod nams zhing / /
bskrun pas 'dren mchog zhabs brtan bdag cag byang chen ma thob bar / /
'bral med rjes bzungs 'gro kun rnam mkhyen sal 'god nus shog /
ces 'tsho byed mkhas pa dge slong dge 'dun don grub kyis ngos kyi 'dra gzugs 'dod lha'i bris thang bzhengs pa'i rgyab yig 'dod smon dgos chul ltar shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
shu b+ha mastu / /
! oM ngal ba sos bka' nyan yang dag shes ser po / /
zhal gcig phyag gnyis gser gri ne'u le 'dzin / /
stong gsum yud myul gser ldan rta mchog chibs / /
'khor bcas dam ldan mchod pa'i gnas 'dir gshegs / /
phyi nang mchod sprin bum bzang rta mchog pa / /
'dod yon sman sna rdzas brgyad rin chen bdun / /
spyan gzigs dam rdzas gtor tshogs gser skyems sogs / /
byin brlabs chos skyong 'khor bcas dgyes phyir 'bul / /
rnal 'byor dpon slob dgon gnas 'khor bcas rnams / /
bu bzhin rtag tu bsrung skyob g.yel med dang / /
bshad sgrub dpal 'byor bstan pa'i byang sogs / /
'phel zhing rgyas pa'i 'phrin las sgrub par mdzod / /
ces rtan ga ri khung chos bdag la mchod bstod 'di ni drung ram pa ye shes bshes gnyen gyis nan gyis bskul ngor chos smra ba'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / / / /
! swasti /
rnam 'dren kun gyi mkhyen brtse nus pa'i rtsal / /
ma lus legs par 'doms pa rgyal ba'i sras / /
thog med dus nas gang 'tshams thabs mkhas pa'i / /
lha gcig pad dkar 'chang la gsol ba 'debs / /
blo chen gang des thugs bskyed bden pa'i stobs / /
ngo mtshar sgyu 'phrul bzang po'i dur smrig gar / /
bsil ljongs skal bzang gdul bya'i mgon skyabs dpung / /
bskal brgya mtsho'i bar du zhabs brtan shog /
phul byung blo gros bzang bos thub pa'i lugs / /
tshul khrims yon tan kun gzhi'i mdzod bzungs nas / /
khrims ldan la bkod skal bzang slob ma'i tshogs / /
rgya mtsho'i gos can 'gengs mdzad zhabs brtan shog /
blo bzang rgyal ba'i gzhung lugs padmo'i tshal / /
thugs rje'i 'od stong 'bar bas legs bzhad cing / /
zab don sbrang rtsis skal bzang bung ba'i tshogs / /
'tsho mdzad rgya mtsho lta bur g.yo med shog /
rgyal kun mkhyen brtse'i dri bzhon gyis drangs pa'i / /
snying stobs dar drag tsan+dan dri bsung gis / /
snyigs bdo'i skye dgu'i tsha gdung sel ba'i mchog /
mtshungs med dpal ldan bla mar gsol ba 'debs / /
rab 'byams rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i dgongs pa'i bcud / /
thugs su chud pa'i zab lam rim gnyis kyi / /
rnal 'byor mthar phyin dkyil 'khor bye ba'i bdag /
zung 'jug dang po'i mgon por gsol ba 'debs / /
'chi med lam ltar yangs pa'i mkhyen dpyod kyis / /
'chad rtsod rtsom pas 'jam mgon bla ma yi / /
lung rtogs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i mchog /
'gyur med rdo rje'i @# / /
khril rtag bzhugs gsol / /
rgyal ba'i 'phrin las zhwa ser bstan pa'i gdugs / /
legs 'degs lugs gnyis skyong ba mi yi bdag /
sku tshe chab srid mnga' thang gong 'phel zhing / /
ljongs 'dir phan dang bde bas khyab par shog /
skyabs mchog rnam gsum thugs rje srung ma'i rtsal / /
lha dang drang srong bden pa'i tshig btsan po / /
rten 'brel slu med mthu yis 'gro ba rnams / /
rdzogs ldan dpal la rol pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces lha dang bcas pa'i 'gro ba yongs kyi skyabs gnas dam pa thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po blo bzang skal bzang rgya mtsho dpal bzang po bstan mi'i dbang po nyid kyang phun du brtan pa bcas kyi bden pa'i mi'i dbang po nyid kyang yun du brtan pa bcas kyi bden pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di ni shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis dang ba'i yid kyis sbyar ba'o / /
sarba mang+galaM / /
! swasti /
blo chen bzang po'i lung rtogs dbang gi rgyal / /
rlabs chen 'phrin las bzang po'i dpal 'bar ba / /
skal bzang gdul bya'i ri skong bla na med / /
dbal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs /
zhes pa 'di ni khal kha dga' ldan bkra shis dge 'phel bcas grwa tshang khag bzhi'i brgyud 'debs gras su er te ni paN+Ti ta no min khang blo bzang dbang chen dpal 'bar la gsol 'debs tshigs bcad gcig dgos zhes bla grwa /
phyag mdzod blo bzang mkhas mchog bcas kyis bskul ngor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis smras so / /
! swasti /
ngag gi dbang phyug gzhon nu'i tshul 'chang ba / /
rnam rol blo bzang rgyal ba gnyis pa yi / /
chos tshul slob tshogs rgya mtshor spel slang du / /
yang srid gsal bar 'byon la gsol ba 'debs / /
gdod nas legs byas du ma las grub pa'i / /
gdul /
bya kun+da'i dga' tshal 'byed pa la / /
bsam bzhin skye srid kun phan gzhon nu can / /
thub bstan nyin mo'i rtse mor rab 'phags shog /
slu med mchog gsum dam pa'i thugs rje dang / /
dam can chos kyi rgyal po mthu rtsal can / /
rtse gcig mos pa'i dad ldan rten 'brel mthus / /
yid la 'dod pa'i re ba skong bar shog /
ces pa 'di yang mdo smad dgon lung bla ma jing si'u chan shi thu'u ba kwan hu thog thu ngag dbang blo bzang chos rgya mtsho'i yang srid myur 'byon gyi gsol 'debs tshigs bcad cig dgos tshul thu'u bkwan chos rje ngag dbang bstan dar dang /
dbon po ngag dbang chos bzang gis nan cher bskul ba ltar shAkya'i dge slong bzang ye shes kyi bgyis ba'o / /
! swasti /
rnam 'dren rgyal ba sras dang bcas rnams kyi / /
mkhyen brtse nus pa'i byin rlabs mthu chen pos / /
blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i / /
yang srid dal 'byor rten bzang myur 'dzin shog /
'gal rkyen bar chad 'khrul pa'i smag rum kun / /
bsangs nas phan bde'i snang ba rgyas byed pa'i / /
thugs rje'i 'od stong gdul bya'i mkhar shar nas / /
skal ldan padmo'i tshil rab rgyas byed shog /
rtag tu bden pa brjod pa rdzogs sangs rgyas / /
de'i gsung bslu ba med pa dam pa'i chos / /
mchod gnas dam ba dge 'dun @# / /
'dus tshogs kyi / /
byin rlabs 'jug la g.yel med bkra shis stsol /
zhes btsan po smin grol ni min han blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho'i yang srid myur 'byon gyi bden pa'i tshig brjod pa 'di ni d+ha'i ching sogs ri dgon thun mong gis bskul ba'i ngor shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba'o / /
! swasti /
'chi med tshe dpag med pa'i snang brnyan yid 'od 'di / /
gus pas mgron sas bskrun pa'i rten 'brel rnam dkar mthus / /
tshe mtha' yas bzhin rje btsun bla ma bskal brgya'i bar / /
rtag bzhugs bdag sogs rjes bzungs 'phrin las dar rgyas shog /
ces pa 'di ni ngos bgrang bya don lnga'i thog ring 'tsho'i rten 'brel du / /
mgron gnyer sa khud pa ye shes bstan 'dzin gyis rgyal ba tshe dpag med kyi snang brnyan khri rgyab bcas bzhengs pa'i smon tshig bskul dor shAkya'i btsun pa blo bzang ye shes kyis sbyar ba mang+galaM / /
b+ha wan+tu / /
! swasti /
ngag gi dbang phyug rje btsun tsong kha pa'i / /
ring lugs ye shes snang bas blo mun sel / /
dam chos dpal 'byor rgya mtshor longs spyod cing / /
'phrin las phyogs bcur spel mdzad zhabs brtan shog /
rnam mang shes bya'i lha lam yangs pa la / /
lung dang rigs pa'i chu 'dzin rab 'khrigs shing / /
zab rgyas chos kyi gru char rgyun mi 'chad / /
'bebs mkhas dpal ldan bla ma zhabs brtan shog /
sangs rgyas de gsung dge 'dun rgyal sras bden / /
mos ldan gsol btab rgyu 'bras slu med mthus / /
rje btsun bla ma zhabs brtan yul phyogs 'dir / /
bde skyid snang ba'i nyi ma cher 'bar shog /
ces pa 'di ni dar rgan bla ma blo bzang bstan 'dzin sogs slob 'khor tshangs mas bskul do dang bstun shAkya'i dge slong blo bzang ye shes kyis smras pa'o / /
! na mo gu ru sh+'+k+ya mu na ye /
'phags yul rdo rje gdan gyi gnas mchog der / /
zas gtsang sras mchog mngon par sangs rgyas tshe / /
gru dang bang rim bzhi po dang ldan pa / /
bdud kun rab bcom byang chub mchod rten che / /
bzhengs pa lta bur mes po'i rnam dkar mthus / /
gser sbyangs las bskrun ngo mtshar bltan sdug /
byin rlabs gzi byin 'od stong rab 'bar ba / /
gnas 'dir bsod nams zhing du legs bzhugs gsol / /

bsod nams rten mchog rnams la dus kun tu / /

de nas /
phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba sras dang rten mchog la / /

mar gyur 'gro rnams mngon mtho nges legs kyi / /

bdag gzhan rnam par dkar ba'i mthu dbung la / /

dge mtshan bdud rtsi'i 'byung gnas gzegs rdul gyis / /

@# / /
srid dang zhi ba ri snang byed 'od po ches / /
phyogs kun mun pa'i smag rum bsal bar shog /
khyad par yul 'di'i lus can mchog dman par / /
dus dang gnas skabs nad mug 'thab rtsod dang / /
mi mthun 'tshe bral kun kyang pha ma ltar / /
rtag tu mdza' zhing byams pa'i sems ldan shog /
d+ha la'i pa'i sa byang chub rdo rje yi / /
rigs rgyud chab 'bangs mnga' thang tshe bsod rgyas / /
'bad med mkho dgu'i 'byor pa lhun grub cing / /
rdzogs ldan dus la 'gran pa'i bkra shis shog /
ces pa 'di yang d+ha la'i ba'i se byang chub rdo rje'i yab mes kyi skabs /

lugs bzang spel la smra mkhas ngag gi dbang / /
